[They are] those who endured patiently and upon their Lord relied.

# 1944

And We sent not before you except men to whom We revealed [Our message]. So ask the people of the message if you do not know.

# 1945

[We sent them] with clear proofs and written ordinances. And We revealed to you the message that you may make clear to the people what was sent down to them and that they might give thought.

# 1946

Then, do those who have planned evil deeds feel secure that Allah will not cause the earth to swallow them or that the punishment will not come upon them from where they do not perceive?

# 1947

Or that He would not seize them during their [usual] activity, and they could not cause failure?

# 1948

Or that He would not seize them gradually [in a state of dread]? But indeed, your Lord is Kind and Merciful.

# 1949

Have they not considered what things Allah has created? Their shadows incline to the right and to the left, prostrating to Allah, while they are humble.

# 1950

And to Allah prostrates whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth of creatures, and the angels [as well], and they are not arrogant.

# 1951

They fear their Lord above them, and they do what they are commanded.

# 1952

And Allah has said, "Do not take for yourselves two deities. He is but one God, so fear only Me."

# 1953

And to Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and the earth, and to Him is [due] worship constantly. Then is it other than Allah that you fear?

# 1954

And whatever you have of favor - it is from Allah. Then when adversity touches you, to Him you cry for help.

# 1955

Then when He removes the adversity from you, at once a party of you associates others with their Lord

# 1956

So they will deny what We have given them. Then enjoy yourselves, for you are going to know.

# 1957

And they assign to what they do not know a portion of that which We have provided them. By Allah, you will surely be questioned about what you used to invent.

# 1958

And they attribute to Allah daughters - exalted is He - and for them is what they desire.

# 1959

And when one of them is informed of [the birth of] a female, his face becomes dark, and he suppresses grief.

# 1960

He hides himself from the people because of the ill of which he has been informed. Should he keep it in humiliation or bury it in the ground? Unquestionably, evil is what they decide.

# 1961

For those who do not believe in the Hereafter is the description of evil; and for Allah is the highest attribute. And He is Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 1962

And if Allah were to impose blame on the people for their wrongdoing, He would not have left upon the earth any creature, but He defers them for a specified term. And when their term has come, they will not remain behind an hour, nor will they precede [it].

# 1963

And they attribute to Allah that which they dislike, and their tongues assert the lie that they will have the best [from Him]. Assuredly, they will have the Fire, and they will be [therein] neglected.

# 1964

By Allah, We did certainly send [messengers] to nations before you, but Satan made their deeds attractive to them. And he is the disbelievers' ally today [as well], and they will have a painful punishment.

# 1965

And We have not revealed to you the Book, [O Muhammad], except for you to make clear to them that wherein they have differed and as guidance and mercy for a people who believe.

# 1966

And Allah has sent down rain from the sky and given life thereby to the earth after its lifelessness. Indeed in that is a sign for a people who listen.

# 1967

And indeed, for you in grazing livestock is a lesson. We give you drink from what is in their bellies - between excretion and blood - pure milk, palatable to drinkers.

# 1968

And from the fruits of the palm trees and grapevines you take intoxicant and good provision. Indeed in that is a sign for a people who reason.

# 1969

And your Lord inspired to the bee, "Take for yourself among the mountains, houses, and among the trees and [in] that which they construct.

# 1970

Then eat from all the fruits and follow the ways of your Lord laid down [for you]." There emerges from their bellies a drink, varying in colors, in which there is healing for people. Indeed in that is a sign for a people who give thought.

# 1971

And Allah created you; then He will take you in death. And among you is he who is reversed to the most decrepit [old] age so that he will not know, after [having had] knowledge, a thing. Indeed, Allah is Knowing and Competent.

# 1972

And Allah has favored some of you over others in provision. But those who were favored would not hand over their provision to those whom their right hands possess so they would be equal to them therein. Then is it the favor of Allah they reject?

# 1973

And Allah has made for you from yourselves mates and has made for you from your mates sons and grandchildren and has provided for you from the good things. Then in falsehood do they believe and in the favor of Allah they disbelieve?

# 1974

And they worship besides Allah that which does not possess for them [the power of] provision from the heavens and the earth at all, and [in fact], they are unable.

# 1975

So do not assert similarities to Allah. Indeed, Allah knows and you do not know.

# 1976

Allah presents an example: a slave [who is] owned and unable to do a thing and he to whom We have provided from Us good provision, so he spends from it secretly and publicly. Can they be equal? Praise to Allah! But most of them do not know.

# 1977

And Allah presents an example of two men, one of them dumb and unable to do a thing, while he is a burden to his guardian. Wherever he directs him, he brings no good. Is he equal to one who commands justice, while he is on a straight path?

# 1978

And to Allah belongs the unseen [aspects] of the heavens and the earth. And the command for the Hour is not but as a glance of the eye or even nearer. Indeed, Allah is over all things competent.

# 1979

And Allah has extracted you from the wombs of your mothers not knowing a thing, and He made for you hearing and vision and intellect that perhaps you would be grateful.

# 1980

Do they not see the birds controlled in the atmosphere of the sky? None holds them up except Allah. Indeed in that are signs for a people who believe.

# 1981

And Allah has made for you from your homes a place of rest and made for you from the hides of the animals tents which you find light on your day of travel and your day of encampment; and from their wool, fur and hair is furnishing and enjoyment for a time.

# 1982

And Allah has made for you, from that which He has created, shadows and has made for you from the mountains, shelters and has made for you garments which protect you from the heat and garments which protect you from your [enemy in] battle. Thus does He complete His favor upon you that you might submit [to Him].

# 1983

But if they turn away, [O Muhammad] - then only upon you is [responsibility for] clear notification.

# 1984

They recognize the favor of Allah; then they deny it. And most of them are disbelievers.

# 1985

And [mention] the Day when We will resurrect from every nation a witness. Then it will not be permitted to the disbelievers [to apologize or make excuses], nor will they be asked to appease [Allah].

# 1986

And when those who wronged see the punishment, it will not be lightened for them, nor will they be reprieved.

# 1987

And when those who associated others with Allah see their "partners," they will say," Our Lord, these are our partners [to You] whom we used to invoke besides You." But they will throw at them the statement, "Indeed, you are liars."

# 1988

And they will impart to Allah that Day [their] submission, and lost from them is what they used to invent.

# 1989

Those who disbelieved and averted [others] from the way of Allah - We will increase them in punishment over [their] punishment for what corruption they were causing.

# 1990

And [mention] the Day when We will resurrect among every nation a witness over them from themselves. And We will bring you, [O Muhammad], as a witness over your nation. And We have sent down to you the Book as clarification for all things and as guidance and mercy and good tidings for the Muslims.

# 1991

Indeed, Allah orders justice and good conduct and giving to relatives and forbids immorality and bad conduct and oppression. He admonishes you that perhaps you will be reminded.

# 1992

And fulfill the covenant of Allah when you have taken it, [O believers], and do not break oaths after their confirmation while you have made Allah, over you, a witness. Indeed, Allah knows what you do.

# 1993

And do not be like she who untwisted her spun thread after it was strong [by] taking your oaths as [means of] deceit between you because one community is more plentiful [in number or wealth] than another community. Allah only tries you thereby. And He will surely make clear to you on the Day of Resurrection that over which you used to differ.

# 1994

And if Allah had willed, He could have made you [of] one religion, but He causes to stray whom He wills and guides whom He wills. And you will surely be questioned about what you used to do.

# 1995

And do not take your oaths as [means of] deceit between you, lest a foot slip after it was [once] firm, and you would taste evil [in this world] for what [people] you diverted from the way of Allah, and you would have [in the Hereafter] a great punishment.

# 1996

And do not exchange the covenant of Allah for a small price. Indeed, what is with Allah is best for you, if only you could know.

# 1997

Whatever you have will end, but what Allah has is lasting. And We will surely give those who were patient their reward according to the best of what they used to do.

# 1998

Whoever does righteousness, whether male or female, while he is a believer - We will surely cause him to live a good life, and We will surely give them their reward [in the Hereafter] according to the best of what they used to do.

# 1999

So when you recite the Qur'an, [first] seek refuge in Allah from Satan, the expelled [from His mercy].

# 2000

Indeed, there is for him no authority over those who have believed and rely upon their Lord.

# 2001

His authority is only over those who take him as an ally and those who through him associate others with Allah.

# 2002

And when We substitute a verse in place of a verse - and Allah is most knowing of what He sends down - they say, "You, [O Muhammad], are but an inventor [of lies]." But most of them do not know.

# 2003

Say, [O Muhammad], "The Pure Spirit has brought it down from your Lord in truth to make firm those who believe and as guidance and good tidings to the Muslims."

# 2004

And We certainly know that they say, "It is only a human being who teaches the Prophet." The tongue of the one they refer to is foreign, and this Qur'an is [in] a clear Arabic language.

# 2005

Indeed, those who do not believe in the verses of Allah - Allah will not guide them, and for them is a painful punishment.

# 2006

They only invent falsehood who do not believe in the verses of Allah, and it is those who are the liars.

# 2007

Whoever disbelieves in Allah after his belief... except for one who is forced [to renounce his religion] while his heart is secure in faith. But those who [willingly] open their breasts to disbelief, upon them is wrath from Allah, and for them is a great punishment;

# 2008

That is because they preferred the worldly life over the Hereafter and that Allah does not guide the disbelieving people.

# 2009

Those are the ones over whose hearts and hearing and vision Allah has sealed, and it is those who are the heedless.

# 2010

Assuredly, it is they, in the Hereafter, who will be the losers.

# 2011

Then, indeed your Lord, to those who emigrated after they had been compelled [to renounce their religion] and thereafter fought [for the cause of Allah] and were patient - indeed, your Lord, after that, is Forgiving and Merciful

# 2012

On the Day when every soul will come disputing for itself, and every soul will be fully compensated for what it did, and they will not be wronged.

# 2013

And Allah presents an example: a city which was safe and secure, its provision coming to it in abundance from every location, but it denied the favors of Allah. So Allah made it taste the envelopment of hunger and fear for what they had been doing.

# 2014

And there had certainly come to them a Messenger from among themselves, but they denied him; so punishment overtook them while they were wrongdoers.

# 2015

Then eat of what Allah has provided for you [which is] lawful and good. And be grateful for the favor of Allah, if it is [indeed] Him that you worship.

# 2016

He has only forbidden to you dead animals, blood, the flesh of swine, and that which has been dedicated to other than Allah. But whoever is forced [by necessity], neither desiring [it] nor transgressing [its limit] - then indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 2017

And do not say about what your tongues assert of untruth, "This is lawful and this is unlawful," to invent falsehood about Allah. Indeed, those who invent falsehood about Allah will not succeed.

# 2018

[It is but] a brief enjoyment, and they will have a painful punishment.

# 2019

And to those who are Jews We have prohibited that which We related to you before. And We did not wrong them [thereby], but they were wronging themselves.

# 2020

Then, indeed your Lord, to those who have done wrong out of ignorance and then repent after that and correct themselves - indeed, your Lord, thereafter, is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 2021

Indeed, Abraham was a [comprehensive] leader, devoutly obedient to Allah, inclining toward truth, and he was not of those who associate others with Allah.

# 2022

[He was] grateful for His favors. Allah chose him and guided him to a straight path.

# 2023

And We gave him good in this world, and indeed, in the Hereafter he will be among the righteous.

# 2024

Then We revealed to you, [O Muhammad], to follow the religion of Abraham, inclining toward truth; and he was not of those who associate with Allah.

# 2025

The sabbath was only appointed for those who differed over it. And indeed, your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which they used to differ.

# 2026

Invite to the way of your Lord with wisdom and good instruction, and argue with them in a way that is best. Indeed, your Lord is most knowing of who has strayed from His way, and He is most knowing of who is [rightly] guided.

# 2027

And if you punish [an enemy, O believers], punish with an equivalent of that with which you were harmed. But if you are patient - it is better for those who are patient.

# 2028

And be patient, [O Muhammad], and your patience is not but through Allah. And do not grieve over them and do not be in distress over what they conspire.

# 2029

Indeed, Allah is with those who fear Him and those who are doers of good.

# 2030

Exalted is He who took His Servant by night from al-Masjid al-Haram to al-Masjid al-Aqsa, whose surroundings We have blessed, to show him of Our signs. Indeed, He is the Hearing, the Seeing.

# 2031

And We gave Moses the Scripture and made it a guidance for the Children of Israel that you not take other than Me as Disposer of affairs,

# 2032

O descendants of those We carried [in the ship] with Noah. Indeed, he was a grateful servant.

# 2033

And We conveyed to the Children of Israel in the Scripture that, "You will surely cause corruption on the earth twice, and you will surely reach [a degree of] great haughtiness.

# 2034

So when the [time of] promise came for the first of them, We sent against you servants of Ours - those of great military might, and they probed [even] into the homes, and it was a promise fulfilled.

# 2035

Then We gave back to you a return victory over them. And We reinforced you with wealth and sons and made you more numerous in manpower

# 2036

[And said], "If you do good, you do good for yourselves; and if you do evil, [you do it] to yourselves." Then when the final promise came, [We sent your enemies] to sadden your faces and to enter the temple in Jerusalem, as they entered it the first time, and to destroy what they had taken over with [total] destruction.

# 2037

[Then Allah said], "It is expected, [if you repent], that your Lord will have mercy upon you. But if you return [to sin], We will return [to punishment]. And We have made Hell, for the disbelievers, a prison-bed."

# 2038

Indeed, this Qur'an guides to that which is most suitable and gives good tidings to the believers who do righteous deeds that they will have a great reward.

# 2039

And that those who do not believe in the Hereafter - We have prepared for them a painful punishment.

# 2040

And man supplicates for evil as he supplicates for good, and man is ever hasty.

# 2041

And We have made the night and day two signs, and We erased the sign of the night and made the sign of the day visible that you may seek bounty from your Lord and may know the number of years and the account [of time]. And everything We have set out in detail.

# 2042

And [for] every person We have imposed his fate upon his neck, and We will produce for him on the Day of Resurrection a record which he will encounter spread open.

# 2043

[It will be said], "Read your record. Sufficient is yourself against you this Day as accountant."

# 2044

Whoever is guided is only guided for [the benefit of] his soul. And whoever errs only errs against it. And no bearer of burdens will bear the burden of another. And never would We punish until We sent a messenger.

# 2045

And when We intend to destroy a city, We command its affluent but they defiantly disobey therein; so the word comes into effect upon it, and We destroy it with [complete] destruction.

# 2046

And how many have We destroyed from the generations after Noah. And sufficient is your Lord, concerning the sins of His servants, as Acquainted and Seeing.

# 2047

Whoever should desire the immediate - We hasten for him from it what We will to whom We intend. Then We have made for him Hell, which he will [enter to] burn, censured and banished.

# 2048

But whoever desires the Hereafter and exerts the effort due to it while he is a believer - it is those whose effort is ever appreciated [by Allah].

# 2049

To each [category] We extend - to these and to those - from the gift of your Lord. And never has the gift of your Lord been restricted.

# 2050

Look how We have favored [in provision] some of them over others. But the Hereafter is greater in degrees [of difference] and greater in distinction.

# 2051

Do not make [as equal] with Allah another deity and [thereby] become censured and forsaken.

# 2052

And your Lord has decreed that you not worship except Him, and to parents, good treatment. Whether one or both of them reach old age [while] with you, say not to them [so much as], "uff," and do not repel them but speak to them a noble word.

# 2053

And lower to them the wing of humility out of mercy and say, "My Lord, have mercy upon them as they brought me up [when I was] small."

# 2054

Your Lord is most knowing of what is within yourselves. If you should be righteous [in intention] - then indeed He is ever, to the often returning [to Him], Forgiving.

# 2055

And give the relative his right, and [also] the poor and the traveler, and do not spend wastefully.

# 2056

Indeed, the wasteful are brothers of the devils, and ever has Satan been to his Lord ungrateful.

# 2057

And if you [must] turn away from the needy awaiting mercy from your Lord which you expect, then speak to them a gentle word.

# 2058

And do not make your hand [as] chained to your neck or extend it completely and [thereby] become blamed and insolvent.

# 2059

Indeed, your Lord extends provision for whom He wills and restricts [it]. Indeed He is ever, concerning His servants, Acquainted and Seeing.

# 2060

And do not kill your children for fear of poverty. We provide for them and for you. Indeed, their killing is ever a great sin.

# 2061

And do not approach unlawful sexual intercourse. Indeed, it is ever an immorality and is evil as a way.

# 2062

And do not kill the soul which Allah has forbidden, except by right. And whoever is killed unjustly - We have given his heir authority, but let him not exceed limits in [the matter of] taking life. Indeed, he has been supported [by the law].

# 2063

And do not approach the property of an orphan, except in the way that is best, until he reaches maturity. And fulfill [every] commitment. Indeed, the commitment is ever [that about which one will be] questioned.

# 2064

And give full measure when you measure, and weigh with an even balance. That is the best [way] and best in result.

# 2065

And do not pursue that of which you have no knowledge. Indeed, the hearing, the sight and the heart - about all those [one] will be questioned.

# 2066

And do not walk upon the earth exultantly. Indeed, you will never tear the earth [apart], and you will never reach the mountains in height.

# 2067

All that - its evil is ever, in the sight of your Lord, detested.

# 2068

That is from what your Lord has revealed to you, [O Muhammad], of wisdom. And, [O mankind], do not make [as equal] with Allah another deity, lest you be thrown into Hell, blamed and banished.

# 2069

Then, has your Lord chosen you for [having] sons and taken from among the angels daughters? Indeed, you say a grave saying.

# 2070

And We have certainly diversified [the contents] in this Qur'an that mankind may be reminded, but it does not increase the disbelievers except in aversion.

# 2071

Say, [O Muhammad], "If there had been with Him [other] gods, as they say, then they [each] would have sought to the Owner of the Throne a way."

# 2072

Exalted is He and high above what they say by great sublimity.

# 2073

The seven heavens and the earth and whatever is in them exalt Him. And there is not a thing except that it exalts [Allah] by His praise, but you do not understand their [way of] exalting. Indeed, He is ever Forbearing and Forgiving.

# 2074

And when you recite the Qur'an, We put between you and those who do not believe in the Hereafter a concealed partition.

# 2075

And We have placed over their hearts coverings, lest they understand it, and in their ears deafness. And when you mention your Lord alone in the Qur'an, they turn back in aversion.

# 2076

We are most knowing of how they listen to it when they listen to you and [of] when they are in private conversation, when the wrongdoers say, "You follow not but a man affected by magic."

# 2077

Look how they strike for you comparisons; but they have strayed, so they cannot [find] a way.

# 2078

And they say, "When we are bones and crumbled particles, will we [truly] be resurrected as a new creation?"

# 2079

Say, "Be you stones or iron

# 2080

Or [any] creation of that which is great within your breasts." And they will say, "Who will restore us?" Say, "He who brought you forth the first time." Then they will nod their heads toward you and say, "When is that?" Say, "Perhaps it will be soon -

# 2081

On the Day He will call you and you will respond with praise of Him and think that you had not remained [in the world] except for a little."

# 2082

And tell My servants to say that which is best. Indeed, Satan induces [dissension] among them. Indeed Satan is ever, to mankind, a clear enemy.

# 2083

Your Lord is most knowing of you. If He wills, He will have mercy upon you; or if He wills, He will punish you. And We have not sent you, [O Muhammad], over them as a manager.

# 2084

And your Lord is most knowing of whoever is in the heavens and the earth. And We have made some of the prophets exceed others [in various ways], and to David We gave the book [of Psalms].

# 2085

Say, "Invoke those you have claimed [as gods] besides Him, for they do not possess the [ability for] removal of adversity from you or [for its] transfer [to someone else]."

# 2086

Those whom they invoke seek means of access to their Lord, [striving as to] which of them would be nearest, and they hope for His mercy and fear His punishment. Indeed, the punishment of your Lord is ever feared.

# 2087

And there is no city but that We will destroy it before the Day of Resurrection or punish it with a severe punishment. That has ever been in the Register inscribed.

# 2088

And nothing has prevented Us from sending signs except that the former peoples denied them. And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged her. And We send not the signs except as a warning.

# 2089

And [remember, O Muhammad], when We told you, "Indeed, your Lord has encompassed the people." And We did not make the sight which We showed you except as a trial for the people, as was the accursed tree [mentioned] in the Qur'an. And We threaten them, but it increases them not except in great transgression.

# 2090

And [mention] when We said to the angles, "Prostrate to Adam," and they prostrated, except for Iblees. He said, "Should I prostrate to one You created from clay?"

# 2091

[Iblees] said, "Do You see this one whom You have honored above me? If You delay me until the Day of Resurrection, I will surely destroy his descendants, except for a few."

# 2092

[Allah] said, "Go, for whoever of them follows you, indeed Hell will be the recompense of you - an ample recompense.

# 2093

And incite [to senselessness] whoever you can among them with your voice and assault them with your horses and foot soldiers and become a partner in their wealth and their children and promise them." But Satan does not promise them except delusion.

# 2094

Indeed, over My [believing] servants there is for you no authority. And sufficient is your Lord as Disposer of affairs.

# 2095

It is your Lord who drives the ship for you through the sea that you may seek of His bounty. Indeed, He is ever, to you, Merciful.

# 2096

And when adversity touches you at sea, lost are [all] those you invoke except for Him. But when He delivers you to the land, you turn away [from Him]. And ever is man ungrateful.

# 2097

Then do you feel secure that [instead] He will not cause a part of the land to swallow you or send against you a storm of stones? Then you would not find for yourselves an advocate.

# 2098

Or do you feel secure that He will not send you back into the sea another time and send upon you a hurricane of wind and drown you for what you denied? Then you would not find for yourselves against Us an avenger.

# 2099

And We have certainly honored the children of Adam and carried them on the land and sea and provided for them of the good things and preferred them over much of what We have created, with [definite] preference.

# 2100

[Mention, O Muhammad], the Day We will call forth every people with their record [of deeds]. Then whoever is given his record in his right hand - those will read their records, and injustice will not be done to them, [even] as much as a thread [inside the date seed].

# 2101

And whoever is blind in this [life] will be blind in the Hereafter and more astray in way.

# 2102

And indeed, they were about to tempt you away from that which We revealed to you in order to [make] you invent about Us something else; and then they would have taken you as a friend.

# 2103

And if We had not strengthened you, you would have almost inclined to them a little.

# 2104

Then [if you had], We would have made you taste double [punishment in] life and double [after] death. Then you would not find for yourself against Us a helper.

# 2105

And indeed, they were about to drive you from the land to evict you therefrom. And then [when they do], they will not remain [there] after you, except for a little.

# 2106

[That is Our] established way for those We had sent before you of Our messengers; and you will not find in Our way any alteration.

# 2107

Establish prayer at the decline of the sun [from its meridian] until the darkness of the night and [also] the Qur'an of dawn. Indeed, the recitation of dawn is ever witnessed.

# 2108

And from [part of] the night, pray with it as additional [worship] for you; it is expected that your Lord will resurrect you to a praised station.

# 2109

And say, "My Lord, cause me to enter a sound entrance and to exit a sound exit and grant me from Yourself a supporting authority."

# 2110

And say, "Truth has come, and falsehood has departed. Indeed is falsehood, [by nature], ever bound to depart."

# 2111

And We send down of the Qur'an that which is healing and mercy for the believers, but it does not increase the wrongdoers except in loss.

# 2112

And when We bestow favor upon the disbeliever, he turns away and distances himself; and when evil touches him, he is ever despairing.

# 2113

Say, "Each works according to his manner, but your Lord is most knowing of who is best guided in way."

# 2114

And they ask you, [O Muhammad], about the soul. Say, "The soul is of the affair of my Lord. And mankind have not been given of knowledge except a little."

# 2115

And if We willed, We could surely do away with that which We revealed to you. Then you would not find for yourself concerning it an advocate against Us.

# 2116

Except [We have left it with you] as a mercy from your Lord. Indeed, His favor upon you has ever been great.

# 2117

Say, "If mankind and the jinn gathered in order to produce the like of this Qur'an, they could not produce the like of it, even if they were to each other assistants."

# 2118

And We have certainly diversified for the people in this Qur'an from every [kind] of example, but most of the people refused [anything] except disbelief.

# 2119

And they say, "We will not believe you until you break open for us from the ground a spring.

# 2120

Or [until] you have a garden of palm tress and grapes and make rivers gush forth within them in force [and abundance]

# 2121

Or you make the heaven fall upon us in fragments as you have claimed or you bring Allah and the angels before [us]

# 2122

Or you have a house of gold or you ascend into the sky. And [even then], we will not believe in your ascension until you bring down to us a book we may read." Say, "Exalted is my Lord! Was I ever but a human messenger?"

# 2123

And what prevented the people from believing when guidance came to them except that they said, "Has Allah sent a human messenger?"

# 2124

Say, "If there were upon the earth angels walking securely, We would have sent down to them from the heaven an angel [as a] messenger."

# 2125

Say, "Sufficient is Allah as Witness between me and you. Indeed he is ever, concerning His servants, Acquainted and Seeing."

# 2126

And whoever Allah guides - he is the [rightly] guided; and whoever He sends astray - you will never find for them protectors besides Him, and We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection [fallen] on their faces - blind, dumb and deaf. Their refuge is Hell; every time it subsides We increase them in blazing fire.

# 2127

That is their recompense because they disbelieved in Our verses and said, "When we are bones and crumbled particles, will we [truly] be resurrected [in] a new creation?"

# 2128

Do they not see that Allah, who created the heavens and earth, is [the one] Able to create the likes of them? And He has appointed for them a term, about which there is no doubt. But the wrongdoers refuse [anything] except disbelief.

# 2129

Say [to them], "If you possessed the depositories of the mercy of my Lord, then you would withhold out of fear of spending." And ever has man been stingy.

# 2130

And We had certainly given Moses nine evident signs, so ask the Children of Israel [about] when he came to them and Pharaoh said to him, "Indeed I think, O Moses, that you are affected by magic."

# 2131

[Moses] said, "You have already known that none has sent down these [signs] except the Lord of the heavens and the earth as evidence, and indeed I think, O Pharaoh, that you are destroyed."

# 2132

So he intended to drive them from the land, but We drowned him and those with him all together.

# 2133

And We said after Pharaoh to the Children of Israel, "Dwell in the land, and when there comes the promise of the Hereafter, We will bring you forth in [one] gathering."

# 2134

And with the truth We have sent the Qur'an down, and with the truth it has descended. And We have not sent you, [O Muhammad], except as a bringer of good tidings and a warner.

# 2135

And [it is] a Qur'an which We have separated [by intervals] that you might recite it to the people over a prolonged period. And We have sent it down progressively.

# 2136

Say, "Believe in it or do not believe. Indeed, those who were given knowledge before it - when it is recited to them, they fall upon their faces in prostration,

# 2137

And they say, "Exalted is our Lord! Indeed, the promise of our Lord has been fulfilled."

# 2138

And they fall upon their faces weeping, and the Qur'an increases them in humble submission.

# 2139

Say, "Call upon Allah or call upon the Most Merciful. Whichever [name] you call - to Him belong the best names." And do not recite [too] loudly in your prayer or [too] quietly but seek between that an [intermediate] way.

# 2140

And say, "Praise to Allah, who has not taken a son and has had no partner in [His] dominion and has no [need of a] protector out of weakness; and glorify Him with [great] glorification."

# 2141

[All] praise is [due] to Allah, who has sent down upon His Servant the Book and has not made therein any deviance.

# 2142

[He has made it] straight, to warn of severe punishment from Him and to give good tidings to the believers who do righteous deeds that they will have a good reward

# 2143

In which they will remain forever

# 2144

And to warn those who say, "Allah has taken a son."

# 2145

They have no knowledge of it, nor had their fathers. Grave is the word that comes out of their mouths; they speak not except a lie.

# 2146

Then perhaps you would kill yourself through grief over them, [O Muhammad], if they do not believe in this message, [and] out of sorrow.

# 2147

Indeed, We have made that which is on the earth adornment for it that We may test them [as to] which of them is best in deed.

# 2148

And indeed, We will make that which is upon it [into] a barren ground.

# 2149

Or have you thought that the companions of the cave and the inscription were, among Our signs, a wonder?

# 2150

[Mention] when the youths retreated to the cave and said, "Our Lord, grant us from Yourself mercy and prepare for us from our affair right guidance."

# 2151

So We cast [a cover of sleep] over their ears within the cave for a number of years.

# 2152

Then We awakened them that We might show which of the two factions was most precise in calculating what [extent] they had remained in time.

# 2153

It is We who relate to you, [O Muhammad], their story in truth. Indeed, they were youths who believed in their Lord, and We increased them in guidance.

# 2154

And We made firm their hearts when they stood up and said, "Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth. Never will we invoke besides Him any deity. We would have certainly spoken, then, an excessive transgression.

# 2155

These, our people, have taken besides Him deities. Why do they not bring for [worship of] them a clear authority? And who is more unjust than one who invents about Allah a lie?"

# 2156

[The youths said to one another], "And when you have withdrawn from them and that which they worship other than Allah, retreat to the cave. Your Lord will spread out for you of His mercy and will prepare for you from your affair facility."

# 2157

And [had you been present], you would see the sun when it rose, inclining away from their cave on the right, and when it set, passing away from them on the left, while they were [laying] within an open space thereof. That was from the signs of Allah. He whom Allah guides is the [rightly] guided, but he whom He leaves astray - never will you find for him a protecting guide.

# 2158

And you would think them awake, while they were asleep. And We turned them to the right and to the left, while their dog stretched his forelegs at the entrance. If you had looked at them, you would have turned from them in flight and been filled by them with terror.

# 2159

And similarly, We awakened them that they might question one another. Said a speaker from among them, "How long have you remained [here]?" They said, "We have remained a day or part of a day." They said, "Your Lord is most knowing of how long you remained. So send one of you with this silver coin of yours to the city and let him look to which is the best of food and bring you provision from it and let him be cautious. And let no one be aware of you.

# 2160

Indeed, if they come to know of you, they will stone you or return you to their religion. And never would you succeed, then - ever."

# 2161

And similarly, We caused them to be found that they [who found them] would know that the promise of Allah is truth and that of the Hour there is no doubt. [That was] when they disputed among themselves about their affair and [then] said, "Construct over them a structure. Their Lord is most knowing about them." Said those who prevailed in the matter, "We will surely take [for ourselves] over them a masjid."

# 2162

They will say there were three, the fourth of them being their dog; and they will say there were five, the sixth of them being their dog - guessing at the unseen; and they will say there were seven, and the eighth of them was their dog. Say, [O Muhammad], "My Lord is most knowing of their number. None knows them except a few. So do not argue about them except with an obvious argument and do not inquire about them among [the speculators] from anyone."

# 2163

And never say of anything, "Indeed, I will do that tomorrow,"

# 2164

Except [when adding], "If Allah wills." And remember your Lord when you forget [it] and say, "Perhaps my Lord will guide me to what is nearer than this to right conduct."

# 2165

And they remained in their cave for three hundred years and exceeded by nine.

# 2166

Say, "Allah is most knowing of how long they remained. He has [knowledge of] the unseen [aspects] of the heavens and the earth. How Seeing is He and how Hearing! They have not besides Him any protector, and He shares not His legislation with anyone."

# 2167

And recite, [O Muhammad], what has been revealed to you of the Book of your Lord. There is no changer of His words, and never will you find in other than Him a refuge.

# 2168

And keep yourself patient [by being] with those who call upon their Lord in the morning and the evening, seeking His countenance. And let not your eyes pass beyond them, desiring adornments of the worldly life, and do not obey one whose heart We have made heedless of Our remembrance and who follows his desire and whose affair is ever [in] neglect.

# 2169

And say, "The truth is from your Lord, so whoever wills - let him believe; and whoever wills - let him disbelieve." Indeed, We have prepared for the wrongdoers a fire whose walls will surround them. And if they call for relief, they will be relieved with water like murky oil, which scalds [their] faces. Wretched is the drink, and evil is the resting place.

# 2170

Indeed, those who have believed and done righteous deeds - indeed, We will not allow to be lost the reward of any who did well in deeds.

# 2171

Those will have gardens of perpetual residence; beneath them rivers will flow. They will be adorned therein with bracelets of gold and will wear green garments of fine silk and brocade, reclining therein on adorned couches. Excellent is the reward, and good is the resting place.

# 2172

And present to them an example of two men: We granted to one of them two gardens of grapevines, and We bordered them with palm trees and placed between them [fields of] crops.

# 2173

Each of the two gardens produced its fruit and did not fall short thereof in anything. And We caused to gush forth within them a river.

# 2174

And he had fruit, so he said to his companion while he was conversing with him, "I am greater than you in wealth and mightier in [numbers of] men."

# 2175

And he entered his garden while he was unjust to himself. He said, "I do not think that this will perish - ever.

# 2176

And I do not think the Hour will occur. And even if I should be brought back to my Lord, I will surely find better than this as a return."

# 2177

His companion said to him while he was conversing with him, "Have you disbelieved in He who created you from dust and then from a sperm-drop and then proportioned you [as] a man?

# 2178

But as for me, He is Allah, my Lord, and I do not associate with my Lord anyone.

# 2179

And why did you, when you entered your garden, not say, 'What Allah willed [has occurred]; there is no power except in Allah '? Although you see me less than you in wealth and children,

# 2180

It may be that my Lord will give me [something] better than your garden and will send upon it a calamity from the sky, and it will become a smooth, dusty ground,

# 2181

Or its water will become sunken [into the earth], so you would never be able to seek it."

# 2182

And his fruits were encompassed [by ruin], so he began to turn his hands about [in dismay] over what he had spent on it, while it had collapsed upon its trellises, and said, "Oh, I wish I had not associated with my Lord anyone."

# 2183

And there was for him no company to aid him other than Allah, nor could he defend himself.

# 2184

There the authority is [completely] for Allah, the Truth. He is best in reward and best in outcome.

# 2185

And present to them the example of the life of this world, [its being] like rain which We send down from the sky, and the vegetation of the earth mingles with it and [then] it becomes dry remnants, scattered by the winds. And Allah is ever, over all things, Perfect in Ability.

# 2186

Wealth and children are [but] adornment of the worldly life. But the enduring good deeds are better to your Lord for reward and better for [one's] hope.

# 2187

And [warn of] the Day when We will remove the mountains and you will see the earth prominent, and We will gather them and not leave behind from them anyone.

# 2188

And they will be presented before your Lord in rows, [and He will say], "You have certainly come to Us just as We created you the first time. But you claimed that We would never make for you an appointment."

# 2189

And the record [of deeds] will be placed [open], and you will see the criminals fearful of that within it, and they will say, "Oh, woe to us! What is this book that leaves nothing small or great except that it has enumerated it?" And they will find what they did present [before them]. And your Lord does injustice to no one.

# 2190

And [mention] when We said to the angels, "Prostrate to Adam," and they prostrated, except for Iblees. He was of the jinn and departed from the command of his Lord. Then will you take him and his descendants as allies other than Me while they are enemies to you? Wretched it is for the wrongdoers as an exchange.

# 2191

I did not make them witness to the creation of the heavens and the earth or to the creation of themselves, and I would not have taken the misguiders as assistants.

# 2192

And [warn of] the Day when He will say, "Call 'My partners' whom you claimed," and they will invoke them, but they will not respond to them. And We will put between them [a valley of] destruction.

# 2193

And the criminals will see the Fire and will be certain that they are to fall therein. And they will not find from it a way elsewhere.

# 2194

And We have certainly diversified in this Qur'an for the people from every [kind of] example; but man has ever been, most of anything, [prone to] dispute.

# 2195

And nothing has prevented the people from believing when guidance came to them and from asking forgiveness of their Lord except that there [must] befall them the [accustomed] precedent of the former peoples or that the punishment should come [directly] before them.

# 2196

And We send not the messengers except as bringers of good tidings and warners. And those who disbelieve dispute by [using] falsehood to [attempt to] invalidate thereby the truth and have taken My verses, and that of which they are warned, in ridicule.

# 2197

And who is more unjust than one who is reminded of the verses of his Lord but turns away from them and forgets what his hands have put forth? Indeed, We have placed over their hearts coverings, lest they understand it, and in their ears deafness. And if you invite them to guidance - they will never be guided, then - ever.

# 2198

And your Lord is the Forgiving, full of mercy. If He were to impose blame upon them for what they earned, He would have hastened for them the punishment. Rather, for them is an appointment from which they will never find an escape.

# 2199

And those cities - We destroyed them when they wronged, and We made for their destruction an appointed time.

# 2200

And [mention] when Moses said to his servant, "I will not cease [traveling] until I reach the junction of the two seas or continue for a long period."

# 2201

But when they reached the junction between them, they forgot their fish, and it took its course into the sea, slipping away.

# 2202

So when they had passed beyond it, [Moses] said to his boy, "Bring us our morning meal. We have certainly suffered in this, our journey, [much] fatigue."

# 2203

He said, "Did you see when we retired to the rock? Indeed, I forgot [there] the fish. And none made me forget it except Satan - that I should mention it. And it took its course into the sea amazingly".

# 2204

[Moses] said, "That is what we were seeking." So they returned, following their footprints.

# 2205

And they found a servant from among Our servants to whom we had given mercy from us and had taught him from Us a [certain] knowledge.

# 2206

Moses said to him, "May I follow you on [the condition] that you teach me from what you have been taught of sound judgement?"

# 2207

He said, "Indeed, with me you will never be able to have patience.

# 2208

And how can you have patience for what you do not encompass in knowledge?"

# 2209

[Moses] said, "You will find me, if Allah wills, patient, and I will not disobey you in [any] order."

# 2210

He said, "Then if you follow me, do not ask me about anything until I make to you about it mention."

# 2211

So they set out, until when they had embarked on the ship, al-Khidh r tore it open. [Moses] said, "Have you torn it open to drown its people? You have certainly done a grave thing."

# 2212

[Al-Khidh r] said, "Did I not say that with me you would never be able to have patience?"

# 2213

[Moses] said, "Do not blame me for what I forgot and do not cover me in my matter with difficulty."

# 2214

So they set out, until when they met a boy, al-Khidh r killed him. [Moses] said, "Have you killed a pure soul for other than [having killed] a soul? You have certainly done a deplorable thing."

# 2215

[Al-Khidh r] said, "Did I not tell you that with me you would never be able to have patience?"

# 2216

[Moses] said, "If I should ask you about anything after this, then do not keep me as a companion. You have obtained from me an excuse."

# 2217

So they set out, until when they came to the people of a town, they asked its people for food, but they refused to offer them hospitality. And they found therein a wall about to collapse, so al-Khidh r restored it. [Moses] said, "If you wished, you could have taken for it a payment."

# 2218

[Al-Khidh r] said, "This is parting between me and you. I will inform you of the interpretation of that about which you could not have patience.

# 2219

As for the ship, it belonged to poor people working at sea. So I intended to cause defect in it as there was after them a king who seized every [good] ship by force.

# 2220

And as for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared that he would overburden them by transgression and disbelief.

# 2221

So we intended that their Lord should substitute for them one better than him in purity and nearer to mercy.

# 2222

And as for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the city, and there was beneath it a treasure for them, and their father had been righteous. So your Lord intended that they reach maturity and extract their treasure, as a mercy from your Lord. And I did it not of my own accord. That is the interpretation of that about which you could not have patience."

# 2223

And they ask you, [O Muhammad], about Dhul-Qarnayn. Say, "I will recite to you about him a report."

# 2224

Indeed We established him upon the earth, and We gave him to everything a way.

# 2225

So he followed a way

# 2226

Until, when he reached the setting of the sun, he found it [as if] setting in a spring of dark mud, and he found near it a people. Allah said, "O Dhul-Qarnayn, either you punish [them] or else adopt among them [a way of] goodness."

# 2227

He said, "As for one who wrongs, we will punish him. Then he will be returned to his Lord, and He will punish him with a terrible punishment.

# 2228

But as for one who believes and does righteousness, he will have a reward of Paradise, and we will speak to him from our command with ease."

# 2229

Then he followed a way

# 2230

Until, when he came to the rising of the sun, he found it rising on a people for whom We had not made against it any shield.

# 2231

Thus. And We had encompassed [all] that he had in knowledge.

# 2232

Then he followed a way

# 2233

Until, when he reached [a pass] between two mountains, he found beside them a people who could hardly understand [his] speech.

# 2234

They said, "O Dhul-Qarnayn, indeed Gog and Magog are [great] corrupters in the land. So may we assign for you an expenditure that you might make between us and them a barrier?"

# 2235

He said, "That in which my Lord has established me is better [than what you offer], but assist me with strength; I will make between you and them a dam.

# 2236

Bring me sheets of iron" - until, when he had leveled [them] between the two mountain walls, he said, "Blow [with bellows]," until when he had made it [like] fire, he said, "Bring me, that I may pour over it molten copper."

# 2237

So Gog and Magog were unable to pass over it, nor were they able [to effect] in it any penetration.

# 2238

[Dhul-Qarnayn] said, "This is a mercy from my Lord; but when the promise of my Lord comes, He will make it level, and ever is the promise of my Lord true."

# 2239

And We will leave them that day surging over each other, and [then] the Horn will be blown, and We will assemble them in [one] assembly.

# 2240

And We will present Hell that Day to the Disbelievers, on display -

# 2241

Those whose eyes had been within a cover [removed] from My remembrance, and they were not able to hear.

# 2242

Then do those who disbelieve think that they can take My servants instead of Me as allies? Indeed, We have prepared Hell for the disbelievers as a lodging.

# 2243

Say, [O Muhammad], "Shall we [believers] inform you of the greatest losers as to [their] deeds?

# 2244

[They are] those whose effort is lost in worldly life, while they think that they are doing well in work."

# 2245

Those are the ones who disbelieve in the verses of their Lord and in [their] meeting Him, so their deeds have become worthless; and We will not assign to them on the Day of Resurrection any importance.

# 2246

That is their recompense - Hell - for what they denied and [because] they took My signs and My messengers in ridicule.

# 2247

Indeed, those who have believed and done righteous deeds - they will have the Gardens of Paradise as a lodging,

# 2248

Wherein they abide eternally. They will not desire from it any transfer.

# 2249

Say, "If the sea were ink for [writing] the words of my Lord, the sea would be exhausted before the words of my Lord were exhausted, even if We brought the like of it as a supplement."

# 2250

Say, "I am only a man like you, to whom has been revealed that your god is one God. So whoever would hope for the meeting with his Lord - let him do righteous work and not associate in the worship of his Lord anyone."

# 2251

Kaf, Ha, Ya, 'Ayn, Sad.

# 2252

[This is] a mention of the mercy of your Lord to His servant Zechariah

# 2253

When he called to his Lord a private supplication.

# 2254

He said, "My Lord, indeed my bones have weakened, and my head has filled with white, and never have I been in my supplication to You, my Lord, unhappy.

# 2255

And indeed, I fear the successors after me, and my wife has been barren, so give me from Yourself an heir

# 2256

Who will inherit me and inherit from the family of Jacob. And make him, my Lord, pleasing [to You]."

# 2257

[He was told], "O Zechariah, indeed We give you good tidings of a boy whose name will be John. We have not assigned to any before [this] name."

# 2258

He said, "My Lord, how will I have a boy when my wife has been barren and I have reached extreme old age?"

# 2259

[An angel] said, "Thus [it will be]; your Lord says, 'It is easy for Me, for I created you before, while you were nothing.' "

# 2260

[Zechariah] said, "My Lord, make for me a sign." He said, "Your sign is that you will not speak to the people for three nights, [being] sound."

# 2261

So he came out to his people from the prayer chamber and signaled to them to exalt [Allah] in the morning and afternoon.

# 2262

[Allah] said, "O John, take the Scripture with determination." And We gave him judgement [while yet] a boy

# 2263

And affection from Us and purity, and he was fearing of Allah

# 2264

And dutiful to his parents, and he was not a disobedient tyrant.

# 2265

And peace be upon him the day he was born and the day he dies and the day he is raised alive.

# 2266

And mention, [O Muhammad], in the Book [the story of] Mary, when she withdrew from her family to a place toward the east.

# 2267

And she took, in seclusion from them, a screen. Then We sent to her Our Angel, and he represented himself to her as a well-proportioned man.

# 2268

She said, "Indeed, I seek refuge in the Most Merciful from you, [so leave me], if you should be fearing of Allah."

# 2269

He said, "I am only the messenger of your Lord to give you [news of] a pure boy."

# 2270

She said, "How can I have a boy while no man has touched me and I have not been unchaste?"

# 2271

He said, "Thus [it will be]; your Lord says, 'It is easy for Me, and We will make him a sign to the people and a mercy from Us. And it is a matter [already] decreed.' "

# 2272

So she conceived him, and she withdrew with him to a remote place.

# 2273

And the pains of childbirth drove her to the trunk of a palm tree. She said, "Oh, I wish I had died before this and was in oblivion, forgotten."

# 2274

But he called her from below her, "Do not grieve; your Lord has provided beneath you a stream.

# 2275

And shake toward you the trunk of the palm tree; it will drop upon you ripe, fresh dates.

# 2276

So eat and drink and be contented. And if you see from among humanity anyone, say, 'Indeed, I have vowed to the Most Merciful abstention, so I will not speak today to [any] man.' "

# 2277

Then she brought him to her people, carrying him. They said, "O Mary, you have certainly done a thing unprecedented.

# 2278

O sister of Aaron, your father was not a man of evil, nor was your mother unchaste."

# 2279

So she pointed to him. They said, "How can we speak to one who is in the cradle a child?"

# 2280

[Jesus] said, "Indeed, I am the servant of Allah. He has given me the Scripture and made me a prophet.

# 2281

And He has made me blessed wherever I am and has enjoined upon me prayer and zakah as long as I remain alive

# 2282

And [made me] dutiful to my mother, and He has not made me a wretched tyrant.

# 2283

And peace is on me the day I was born and the day I will die and the day I am raised alive."

# 2284

That is Jesus, the son of Mary - the word of truth about which they are in dispute.

# 2285

It is not [befitting] for Allah to take a son; exalted is He! When He decrees an affair, He only says to it, "Be," and it is.

# 2286

[Jesus said], "And indeed, Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. That is a straight path."

# 2287

Then the factions differed [concerning Jesus] from among them, so woe to those who disbelieved - from the scene of a tremendous Day.

# 2288

How [clearly] they will hear and see the Day they come to Us, but the wrongdoers today are in clear error.

# 2289

And warn them, [O Muhammad], of the Day of Regret, when the matter will be concluded; and [yet], they are in [a state of] heedlessness, and they do not believe.

# 2290

Indeed, it is We who will inherit the earth and whoever is on it, and to Us they will be returned.

# 2291

And mention in the Book [the story of] Abraham. Indeed, he was a man of truth and a prophet.

# 2292

[Mention] when he said to his father, "O my father, why do you worship that which does not hear and does not see and will not benefit you at all?

# 2293

O my father, indeed there has come to me of knowledge that which has not come to you, so follow me; I will guide you to an even path.

# 2294

O my father, do not worship Satan. Indeed Satan has ever been, to the Most Merciful, disobedient.

# 2295

O my father, indeed I fear that there will touch you a punishment from the Most Merciful so you would be to Satan a companion [in Hellfire]."

# 2296

[His father] said, "Have you no desire for my gods, O Abraham? If you do not desist, I will surely stone you, so avoid me a prolonged time."

# 2297

[Abraham] said, "Peace will be upon you. I will ask forgiveness for you of my Lord. Indeed, He is ever gracious to me.

# 2298

And I will leave you and those you invoke other than Allah and will invoke my Lord. I expect that I will not be in invocation to my Lord unhappy."

# 2299

So when he had left them and those they worshipped other than Allah, We gave him Isaac and Jacob, and each [of them] We made a prophet.

# 2300

And We gave them of Our mercy, and we made for them a reputation of high honor.

# 2301

And mention in the Book, Moses. Indeed, he was chosen, and he was a messenger and a prophet.

# 2302

And We called him from the side of the mount at [his] right and brought him near, confiding [to him].

# 2303

And We gave him out of Our mercy his brother Aaron as a prophet.

# 2304

And mention in the Book, Ishmael. Indeed, he was true to his promise, and he was a messenger and a prophet.

# 2305

And he used to enjoin on his people prayer and zakah and was to his Lord pleasing.

# 2306

And mention in the Book, Idrees. Indeed, he was a man of truth and a prophet.

# 2307

And We raised him to a high station.

# 2308

Those were the ones upon whom Allah bestowed favor from among the prophets of the descendants of Adam and of those We carried [in the ship] with Noah, and of the descendants of Abraham and Israel, and of those whom We guided and chose. When the verses of the Most Merciful were recited to them, they fell in prostration and weeping.

# 2309

But there came after them successors who neglected prayer and pursued desires; so they are going to meet evil -

# 2310

Except those who repent, believe and do righteousness; for those will enter Paradise and will not be wronged at all.

# 2311

[Therein are] gardens of perpetual residence which the Most Merciful has promised His servants in the unseen. Indeed, His promise has ever been coming.

# 2312

They will not hear therein any ill speech - only [greetings of] peace - and they will have their provision therein, morning and afternoon.

# 2313

That is Paradise, which We give as inheritance to those of Our servants who were fearing of Allah.

# 2314

[Gabriel said], "And we [angels] descend not except by the order of your Lord. To Him belongs that before us and that behind us and what is in between. And never is your Lord forgetful -

# 2315

Lord of the heavens and the earth and whatever is between them - so worship Him and have patience for His worship. Do you know of any similarity to Him?"

# 2316

And the disbeliever says, "When I have died, am I going to be brought forth alive?"

# 2317

Does man not remember that We created him before, while he was nothing?

# 2318

So by your Lord, We will surely gather them and the devils; then We will bring them to be present around Hell upon their knees.

# 2319

Then We will surely extract from every sect those of them who were worst against the Most Merciful in insolence.

# 2320

Then, surely it is We who are most knowing of those most worthy of burning therein.

# 2321

And there is none of you except he will come to it. This is upon your Lord an inevitability decreed.

# 2322

Then We will save those who feared Allah and leave the wrongdoers within it, on their knees.

# 2323

And when Our verses are recited to them as clear evidences, those who disbelieve say to those who believe, "Which of [our] two parties is best in position and best in association?"

# 2324

And how many a generation have We destroyed before them who were better in possessions and [outward] appearance?

# 2325

Say, "Whoever is in error - let the Most Merciful extend for him an extension [in wealth and time] until, when they see that which they were promised - either punishment [in this world] or the Hour [of resurrection] - they will come to know who is worst in position and weaker in soldiers."

# 2326

And Allah increases those who were guided, in guidance, and the enduring good deeds are better to your Lord for reward and better for recourse.

# 2327

Then, have you seen he who disbelieved in Our verses and said, "I will surely be given wealth and children [in the next life]?"

# 2328

Has he looked into the unseen, or has he taken from the Most Merciful a promise?

# 2329

No! We will record what he says and extend for him from the punishment extensively.

# 2330

And We will inherit him [in] what he mentions, and he will come to Us alone.

# 2331

And they have taken besides Allah [false] deities that they would be for them [a source of] honor.

# 2332

No! Those "gods" will deny their worship of them and will be against them opponents [on the Day of Judgement].

# 2333

Do you not see that We have sent the devils upon the disbelievers, inciting them to [evil] with [constant] incitement?

# 2334

So be not impatient over them. We only count out to them a [limited] number.

# 2335

On the Day We will gather the righteous to the Most Merciful as a delegation

# 2336

And will drive the criminals to Hell in thirst

# 2337

None will have [power of] intercession except he who had taken from the Most Merciful a covenant.

# 2338

And they say, "The Most Merciful has taken [for Himself] a son."

# 2339

You have done an atrocious thing.

# 2340

The heavens almost rupture therefrom and the earth splits open and the mountains collapse in devastation

# 2341

That they attribute to the Most Merciful a son.

# 2342

And it is not appropriate for the Most Merciful that He should take a son.

# 2343

There is no one in the heavens and earth but that he comes to the Most Merciful as a servant.

# 2344

He has enumerated them and counted them a [full] counting.

# 2345

And all of them are coming to Him on the Day of Resurrection alone.

# 2346

Indeed, those who have believed and done righteous deeds - the Most Merciful will appoint for them affection.

# 2347

So, [O Muhammad], We have only made Qur'an easy in the Arabic language that you may give good tidings thereby to the righteous and warn thereby a hostile people.

# 2348

And how many have We destroyed before them of generations? Do you perceive of them anyone or hear from them a sound?

# 2349

Ta, Ha.

# 2350

We have not sent down to you the Qur'an that you be distressed

# 2351

But only as a reminder for those who fear [Allah] -

# 2352

A revelation from He who created the earth and highest heavens,

# 2353

The Most Merciful [who is] above the Throne established.

# 2354

To Him belongs what is in the heavens and what is on the earth and what is between them and what is under the soil.

# 2355

And if you speak aloud - then indeed, He knows the secret and what is [even] more hidden.

# 2356

Allah - there is no deity except Him. To Him belong the best names.

# 2357

And has the story of Moses reached you? -

# 2358

When he saw a fire and said to his family, "Stay here; indeed, I have perceived a fire; perhaps I can bring you a torch or find at the fire some guidance."

# 2359

And when he came to it, he was called, "O Moses,

# 2360

Indeed, I am your Lord, so remove your sandals. Indeed, you are in the sacred valley of Tuwa.

# 2361

And I have chosen you, so listen to what is revealed [to you].

# 2362

Indeed, I am Allah. There is no deity except Me, so worship Me and establish prayer for My remembrance.

# 2363

Indeed, the Hour is coming - I almost conceal it - so that every soul may be recompensed according to that for which it strives.

# 2364

So do not let one avert you from it who does not believe in it and follows his desire, for you [then] would perish.

# 2365

And what is that in your right hand, O Moses?"

# 2366

He said, "It is my staff; I lean upon it, and I bring down leaves for my sheep and I have therein other uses."

# 2367

[Allah] said, "Throw it down, O Moses."

# 2368

So he threw it down, and thereupon it was a snake, moving swiftly.

# 2369

[Allah] said, "Seize it and fear not; We will return it to its former condition.

# 2370

And draw in your hand to your side; it will come out white without disease - another sign,

# 2371

That We may show you [some] of Our greater signs.

# 2372

Go to Pharaoh. Indeed, he has transgressed."

# 2373

[Moses] said, "My Lord, expand for me my breast [with assurance]

# 2374

And ease for me my task

# 2375

And untie the knot from my tongue

# 2376

That they may understand my speech.

# 2377

And appoint for me a minister from my family -

# 2378

Aaron, my brother.

# 2379

Increase through him my strength

# 2380

And let him share my task

# 2381

That we may exalt You much

# 2382

And remember You much.

# 2383

Indeed, You are of us ever Seeing."

# 2384

[Allah] said, "You have been granted your request, O Moses.

# 2385

And We had already conferred favor upon you another time,

# 2386

When We inspired to your mother what We inspired,

# 2387

[Saying], 'Cast him into the chest and cast it into the river, and the river will throw it onto the bank; there will take him an enemy to Me and an enemy to him.' And I bestowed upon you love from Me that you would be brought up under My eye.

# 2388

[And We favored you] when your sister went and said, 'Shall I direct you to someone who will be responsible for him?' So We restored you to your mother that she might be content and not grieve. And you killed someone, but We saved you from retaliation and tried you with a [severe] trial. And you remained [some] years among the people of Madyan. Then you came [here] at the decreed time, O Moses.

# 2389

And I produced you for Myself.

# 2390

Go, you and your brother, with My signs and do not slacken in My remembrance.

# 2391

Go, both of you, to Pharaoh. Indeed, he has transgressed.

# 2392

And speak to him with gentle speech that perhaps he may be reminded or fear [Allah]."

# 2393

They said, "Our Lord, indeed we are afraid that he will hasten [punishment] against us or that he will transgress."

# 2394

[Allah] said, "Fear not. Indeed, I am with you both; I hear and I see.

# 2395

So go to him and say, 'Indeed, we are messengers of your Lord, so send with us the Children of Israel and do not torment them. We have come to you with a sign from your Lord. And peace will be upon he who follows the guidance.

# 2396

Indeed, it has been revealed to us that the punishment will be upon whoever denies and turns away.' "

# 2397

[Pharaoh] said, "So who is the Lord of you two, O Moses?"

# 2398

He said, "Our Lord is He who gave each thing its form and then guided [it]."

# 2399

[Pharaoh] said, "Then what is the case of the former generations?"

# 2400

[Moses] said, "The knowledge thereof is with my Lord in a record. My Lord neither errs nor forgets."

# 2401

[It is He] who has made for you the earth as a bed [spread out] and inserted therein for you roadways and sent down from the sky, rain and produced thereby categories of various plants.

# 2402

Eat [therefrom] and pasture your livestock. Indeed, in that are signs for those of intelligence.

# 2403

From the earth We created you, and into it We will return you, and from it We will extract you another time.

# 2404

And We certainly showed Pharaoh Our signs - all of them - but he denied and refused.

# 2405

He said, "Have you come to us to drive us out of our land with your magic, O Moses?

# 2406

Then we will surely bring you magic like it, so make between us and you an appointment, which we will not fail to keep and neither will you, in a place assigned."

# 2407

[Moses] said, "Your appointment is on the day of the festival when the people assemble at mid-morning."

# 2408

So Pharaoh went away, put together his plan, and then came [to Moses].

# 2409

Moses said to the magicians summoned by Pharaoh, "Woe to you! Do not invent a lie against Allah or He will exterminate you with a punishment; and he has failed who invents [such falsehood]."

# 2410

So they disputed over their affair among themselves and concealed their private conversation.

# 2411

They said, "Indeed, these are two magicians who want to drive you out of your land with their magic and do away with your most exemplary way.

# 2412

So resolve upon your plan and then come [forward] in line. And he has succeeded today who overcomes."

# 2413

They said, "O Moses, either you throw or we will be the first to throw."

# 2414

He said, "Rather, you throw." And suddenly their ropes and staffs seemed to him from their magic that they were moving [like snakes].

# 2415

And he sensed within himself apprehension, did Moses.

# 2416

Allah said, "Fear not. Indeed, it is you who are superior.

# 2417

And throw what is in your right hand; it will swallow up what they have crafted. What they have crafted is but the trick of a magician, and the magician will not succeed wherever he is."

# 2418

So the magicians fell down in prostration. They said, "We have believed in the Lord of Aaron and Moses."

# 2419

[Pharaoh] said, "You believed him before I gave you permission. Indeed, he is your leader who has taught you magic. So I will surely cut off your hands and your feet on opposite sides, and I will crucify you on the trunks of palm trees, and you will surely know which of us is more severe in [giving] punishment and more enduring."

# 2420

They said, "Never will we prefer you over what has come to us of clear proofs and [over] He who created us. So decree whatever you are to decree. You can only decree for this worldly life.

# 2421

Indeed, we have believed in our Lord that He may forgive us our sins and what you compelled us [to do] of magic. And Allah is better and more enduring."

# 2422

Indeed, whoever comes to his Lord as a criminal - indeed, for him is Hell; he will neither die therein nor live.

# 2423

But whoever comes to Him as a believer having done righteous deeds - for those will be the highest degrees [in position]:

# 2424

Gardens of perpetual residence beneath which rivers flow, wherein they abide eternally. And that is the reward of one who purifies himself.

# 2425

And We had inspired to Moses, "Travel by night with My servants and strike for them a dry path through the sea; you will not fear being overtaken [by Pharaoh] nor be afraid [of drowning]."

# 2426

So Pharaoh pursued them with his soldiers, and there covered them from the sea that which covered them,

# 2427

And Pharaoh led his people astray and did not guide [them].

# 2428

O Children of Israel, We delivered you from your enemy, and We made an appointment with you at the right side of the mount, and We sent down to you manna and quails,

# 2429

[Saying], "Eat from the good things with which We have provided you and do not transgress [or oppress others] therein, lest My anger should descend upon you. And he upon whom My anger descends has certainly fallen."

# 2430

But indeed, I am the Perpetual Forgiver of whoever repents and believes and does righteousness and then continues in guidance.

# 2431

[Allah] said, "And what made you hasten from your people, O Moses?"

# 2432

He said, "They are close upon my tracks, and I hastened to You, my Lord, that You be pleased."

# 2433

[Allah] said, "But indeed, We have tried your people after you [departed], and the Samiri has led them astray."

# 2434

So Moses returned to his people, angry and grieved. He said, "O my people, did your Lord not make you a good promise? Then, was the time [of its fulfillment] too long for you, or did you wish that wrath from your Lord descend upon you, so you broke your promise [of obedience] to me?"

# 2435

They said, "We did not break our promise to you by our will, but we were made to carry burdens from the ornaments of the people [of Pharaoh], so we threw them [into the fire], and thus did the Samiri throw."

# 2436

And he extracted for them [the statue of] a calf which had a lowing sound, and they said, "This is your god and the god of Moses, but he forgot."

# 2437

Did they not see that it could not return to them any speech and that it did not possess for them any harm or benefit?

# 2438

And Aaron had already told them before [the return of Moses], "O my people, you are only being tested by it, and indeed, your Lord is the Most Merciful, so follow me and obey my order."

# 2439

They said, "We will never cease being devoted to the calf until Moses returns to us."

# 2440

[Moses] said, "O Aaron, what prevented you, when you saw them going astray,

# 2441

From following me? Then have you disobeyed my order?"

# 2442

[Aaron] said, "O son of my mother, do not seize [me] by my beard or by my head. Indeed, I feared that you would say, 'You caused division among the Children of Israel, and you did not observe [or await] my word.' "

# 2443

[Moses] said, "And what is your case, O Samiri?"

# 2444

He said, "I saw what they did not see, so I took a handful [of dust] from the track of the messenger and threw it, and thus did my soul entice me."

# 2445

[Moses] said, "Then go. And indeed, it is [decreed] for you in [this] life to say, 'No contact.' And indeed, you have an appointment [in the Hereafter] you will not fail to keep. And look at your 'god' to which you remained devoted. We will surely burn it and blow it into the sea with a blast.

# 2446

Your god is only Allah, except for whom there is no deity. He has encompassed all things in knowledge."

# 2447

Thus, [O Muhammad], We relate to you from the news of what has preceded. And We have certainly given you from Us the Qur'an.

# 2448

Whoever turns away from it - then indeed, he will bear on the Day of Resurrection a burden,

# 2449

[Abiding] eternally therein, and evil it is for them on the Day of Resurrection as a load -

# 2450

The Day the Horn will be blown. And We will gather the criminals, that Day, blue-eyed.

# 2451

They will murmur among themselves, "You remained not but ten [days in the world]."

# 2452

We are most knowing of what they say when the best of them in manner will say, "You remained not but one day."

# 2453

And they ask you about the mountains, so say, "My Lord will blow them away with a blast.

# 2454

And He will leave the earth a level plain;

# 2455

You will not see therein a depression or an elevation."

# 2456

That Day, everyone will follow [the call of] the Caller [with] no deviation therefrom, and [all] voices will be stilled before the Most Merciful, so you will not hear except a whisper [of footsteps].

# 2457

That Day, no intercession will benefit except [that of] one to whom the Most Merciful has given permission and has accepted his word.

# 2458

Allah knows what is [presently] before them and what will be after them, but they do not encompass it in knowledge.

# 2459

And [all] faces will be humbled before the Ever-Living, the Sustainer of existence. And he will have failed who carries injustice.

# 2460

But he who does of righteous deeds while he is a believer - he will neither fear injustice nor deprivation.

# 2461

And thus We have sent it down as an Arabic Qur'an and have diversified therein the warnings that perhaps they will avoid [sin] or it would cause them remembrance.

# 2462

So high [above all] is Allah, the Sovereign, the Truth. And, [O Muhammad], do not hasten with [recitation of] the Qur'an before its revelation is completed to you, and say, "My Lord, increase me in knowledge."

# 2463

And We had already taken a promise from Adam before, but he forgot; and We found not in him determination.

# 2464

And [mention] when We said to the angels, "Prostrate to Adam," and they prostrated, except Iblees; he refused.

# 2465

So We said, "O Adam, indeed this is an enemy to you and to your wife. Then let him not remove you from Paradise so you would suffer.

# 2466

Indeed, it is [promised] for you not to be hungry therein or be unclothed.

# 2467

And indeed, you will not be thirsty therein or be hot from the sun."

# 2468

Then Satan whispered to him; he said, "O Adam, shall I direct you to the tree of eternity and possession that will not deteriorate?"

# 2469

And Adam and his wife ate of it, and their private parts became apparent to them, and they began to fasten over themselves from the leaves of Paradise. And Adam disobeyed his Lord and erred.

# 2470

Then his Lord chose him and turned to him in forgiveness and guided [him].

# 2471

[Allah] said, "Descend from Paradise - all, [your descendants] being enemies to one another. And if there should come to you guidance from Me - then whoever follows My guidance will neither go astray [in the world] nor suffer [in the Hereafter].

# 2472

And whoever turns away from My remembrance - indeed, he will have a depressed life, and We will gather him on the Day of Resurrection blind."

# 2473

He will say, "My Lord, why have you raised me blind while I was [once] seeing?"

# 2474

[Allah] will say, "Thus did Our signs come to you, and you forgot them; and thus will you this Day be forgotten."

# 2475

And thus do We recompense he who transgressed and did not believe in the signs of his Lord. And the punishment of the Hereafter is more severe and more enduring.

# 2476

Then, has it not become clear to them how many generations We destroyed before them as they walk among their dwellings? Indeed in that are signs for those of intelligence.

# 2477

And if not for a word that preceded from your Lord, punishment would have been an obligation [due immediately], and [if not for] a specified term [decreed].

# 2478

So be patient over what they say and exalt [Allah] with praise of your Lord before the rising of the sun and before its setting; and during periods of the night [exalt Him] and at the ends of the day, that you may be satisfied.

# 2479

And do not extend your eyes toward that by which We have given enjoyment to [some] categories of them, [its being but] the splendor of worldly life by which We test them. And the provision of your Lord is better and more enduring.

# 2480
