It is We who have apportioned among them their livelihood in the life of this world and have raised some of them above others in degrees [of rank] that they may make use of one another for service. But the mercy of your Lord is better than whatever they accumulate.

# 4358

And if it were not that the people would become one community [of disbelievers], We would have made for those who disbelieve in the Most Merciful - for their houses - ceilings and stairways of silver upon which to mount

# 4359

And for their houses - doors and couches [of silver] upon which to recline

# 4360

And gold ornament. But all that is not but the enjoyment of worldly life. And the Hereafter with your Lord is for the righteous.

# 4361

And whoever is blinded from remembrance of the Most Merciful - We appoint for him a devil, and he is to him a companion.

# 4362

And indeed, the devils avert them from the way [of guidance] while they think that they are [rightly] guided

# 4363

Until, when he comes to Us [at Judgement], he says [to his companion], "Oh, I wish there was between me and you the distance between the east and west - how wretched a companion."

# 4364

And never will it benefit you that Day, when you have wronged, that you are [all] sharing in the punishment.

# 4365

Then will you make the deaf hear, [O Muhammad], or guide the blind or he who is in clear error?

# 4366

And whether [or not] We take you away [in death], indeed, We will take retribution upon them.

# 4367

Or whether [or not] We show you that which We have promised them, indeed, We are Perfect in Ability.

# 4368

So adhere to that which is revealed to you. Indeed, you are on a straight path.

# 4369

And indeed, it is a remembrance for you and your people, and you [all] are going to be questioned.

# 4370

And ask those We sent before you of Our messengers; have We made besides the Most Merciful deities to be worshipped?

# 4371

And certainly did We send Moses with Our signs to Pharaoh and his establishment, and he said, "Indeed, I am the messenger of the Lord of the worlds."

# 4372

But when he brought them Our signs, at once they laughed at them.

# 4373

And We showed them not a sign except that it was greater than its sister, and We seized them with affliction that perhaps they might return [to faith].

# 4374

And they said [to Moses], "O magician, invoke for us your Lord by what He has promised you. Indeed, we will be guided."

# 4375

But when We removed from them the affliction, at once they broke their word.

# 4376

And Pharaoh called out among his people; he said, "O my people, does not the kingdom of Egypt belong to me, and these rivers flowing beneath me; then do you not see?

# 4377

Or am I [not] better than this one who is insignificant and hardly makes himself clear?

# 4378

Then why have there not been placed upon him bracelets of gold or come with him the angels in conjunction?"

# 4379

So he bluffed his people, and they obeyed him. Indeed, they were [themselves] a people defiantly disobedient [of Allah].

# 4380

And when they angered Us, We took retribution from them and drowned them all.

# 4381

And We made them a precedent and an example for the later peoples.

# 4382

And when the son of Mary was presented as an example, immediately your people laughed aloud.

# 4383

And they said, "Are your gods better, or is he?" They did not present the comparison except for [mere] argument. But, [in fact], they are a people prone to dispute.

# 4384

Jesus was not but a servant upon whom We bestowed favor, and We made him an example for the Children of Israel.

# 4385

And if We willed, We could have made [instead] of you angels succeeding [one another] on the earth.

# 4386

And indeed, Jesus will be [a sign for] knowledge of the Hour, so be not in doubt of it, and follow Me. This is a straight path.

# 4387

And never let Satan avert you. Indeed, he is to you a clear enemy.

# 4388

And when Jesus brought clear proofs, he said, "I have come to you with wisdom and to make clear to you some of that over which you differ, so fear Allah and obey me.

# 4389

Indeed, Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. This is a straight path."

# 4390

But the denominations from among them differed [and separated], so woe to those who have wronged from the punishment of a painful Day.

# 4391

Are they waiting except for the Hour to come upon them suddenly while they perceive not?

# 4392

Close friends, that Day, will be enemies to each other, except for the righteous

# 4393

[To whom Allah will say], "O My servants, no fear will there be concerning you this Day, nor will you grieve,

# 4394

[You] who believed in Our verses and were Muslims.

# 4395

Enter Paradise, you and your kinds, delighted."

# 4396

Circulated among them will be plates and vessels of gold. And therein is whatever the souls desire and [what] delights the eyes, and you will abide therein eternally.

# 4397

And that is Paradise which you are made to inherit for what you used to do.

# 4398

For you therein is much fruit from which you will eat.

# 4399

Indeed, the criminals will be in the punishment of Hell, abiding eternally.

# 4400

It will not be allowed to subside for them, and they, therein, are in despair.

# 4401

And We did not wrong them, but it was they who were the wrongdoers.

# 4402

And they will call, "O Malik, let your Lord put an end to us!" He will say, "Indeed, you will remain."

# 4403

We had certainly brought you the truth, but most of you, to the truth, were averse.

# 4404

Or have they devised [some] affair? But indeed, We are devising [a plan].

# 4405

Or do they think that We hear not their secrets and their private conversations? Yes, [We do], and Our messengers are with them recording.

# 4406

Say, [O Muhammad], "If the Most Merciful had a son, then I would be the first of [his] worshippers."

# 4407

Exalted is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, Lord of the Throne, above what they describe.

# 4408

So leave them to converse vainly and amuse themselves until they meet their Day which they are promised.

# 4409

And it is Allah who is [the only] deity in the heaven, and on the earth [the only] deity. And He is the Wise, the Knowing.

# 4410

And blessed is He to whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth and whatever is between them and with whom is knowledge of the Hour and to whom you will be returned.

# 4411

And those they invoke besides Him do not possess [power of] intercession; but only those who testify to the truth [can benefit], and they know.

# 4412

And if you asked them who created them, they would surely say, "Allah." So how are they deluded?

# 4413

And [Allah acknowledges] his saying, "O my Lord, indeed these are a people who do not believe."

# 4414

So turn aside from them and say, "Peace." But they are going to know.

# 4415

Ha, Meem.

# 4416

By the clear Book,

# 4417

Indeed, We sent it down during a blessed night. Indeed, We were to warn [mankind].

# 4418

On that night is made distinct every precise matter -

# 4419

[Every] matter [proceeding] from Us. Indeed, We were to send [a messenger]

# 4420

As mercy from your Lord. Indeed, He is the Hearing, the Knowing.

# 4421

Lord of the heavens and the earth and that between them, if you would be certain.

# 4422

There is no deity except Him; He gives life and causes death. [He is] your Lord and the Lord of your first forefathers.

# 4423

But they are in doubt, amusing themselves.

# 4424

Then watch for the Day when the sky will bring a visible smoke.

# 4425

Covering the people; this is a painful torment.

# 4426

[They will say], "Our Lord, remove from us the torment; indeed, we are believers."

# 4427

How will there be for them a reminder [at that time]? And there had come to them a clear Messenger.

# 4428

Then they turned away from him and said, "[He was] taught [and is] a madman."

# 4429

Indeed, We will remove the torment for a little. Indeed, you [disbelievers] will return [to disbelief].

# 4430

The Day We will strike with the greatest assault, indeed, We will take retribution.

# 4431

And We had already tried before them the people of Pharaoh, and there came to them a noble messenger,

# 4432

[Saying], "Render to me the servants of Allah. Indeed, I am to you a trustworthy messenger,"

# 4433

And [saying], "Be not haughty with Allah. Indeed, I have come to you with clear authority.

# 4434

And indeed, I have sought refuge in my Lord and your Lord, lest you stone me.

# 4435

But if you do not believe me, then leave me alone."

# 4436

And [finally] he called to his Lord that these were a criminal people.

# 4437

[Allah said], "Then set out with My servants by night. Indeed, you are to be pursued.

# 4438

And leave the sea in stillness. Indeed, they are an army to be drowned."

# 4439

How much they left behind of gardens and springs

# 4440

And crops and noble sites

# 4441

And comfort wherein they were amused.

# 4442

Thus. And We caused to inherit it another people.

# 4443

And the heaven and earth wept not for them, nor were they reprieved.

# 4444

And We certainly saved the Children of Israel from the humiliating torment -

# 4445

From Pharaoh. Indeed, he was a haughty one among the transgressors.

# 4446

And We certainly chose them by knowledge over [all] the worlds.

# 4447

And We gave them of signs that in which there was a clear trial.

# 4448

Indeed, these [disbelievers] are saying,

# 4449

"There is not but our first death, and we will not be resurrected.

# 4450

Then bring [back] our forefathers, if you should be truthful."

# 4451

Are they better or the people of Tubba' and those before them? We destroyed them, [for] indeed, they were criminals.

# 4452

And We did not create the heavens and earth and that between them in play.

# 4453

We did not create them except in truth, but most of them do not know.

# 4454

Indeed, the Day of Judgement is the appointed time for them all -

# 4455

The Day when no relation will avail a relation at all, nor will they be helped -

# 4456

Except those [believers] on whom Allah has mercy. Indeed, He is the Exalted in Might, the Merciful.

# 4457

Indeed, the tree of zaqqum

# 4458

Is food for the sinful.

# 4459

Like murky oil, it boils within bellies

# 4460

Like the boiling of scalding water.

# 4461

[It will be commanded], "Seize him and drag him into the midst of the Hellfire,

# 4462

Then pour over his head from the torment of scalding water."

# 4463

[It will be said], "Taste! Indeed, you are the honored, the noble!

# 4464

Indeed, this is what you used to dispute."

# 4465

Indeed, the righteous will be in a secure place;

# 4466

Within gardens and springs,

# 4467

Wearing [garments of] fine silk and brocade, facing each other.

# 4468

Thus. And We will marry them to fair women with large, [beautiful] eyes.

# 4469

They will call therein for every [kind of] fruit - safe and secure.

# 4470

They will not taste death therein except the first death, and He will have protected them from the punishment of Hellfire

# 4471

As bounty from your Lord. That is what is the great attainment.

# 4472

And indeed, We have eased the Qur'an in your tongue that they might be reminded.

# 4473

So watch, [O Muhammad]; indeed, they are watching [for your end].

# 4474

Ha, Meem.

# 4475

The revelation of the Book is from Allah, the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 4476

Indeed, within the heavens and earth are signs for the believers.

# 4477

And in the creation of yourselves and what He disperses of moving creatures are signs for people who are certain [in faith].

# 4478

And [in] the alternation of night and day and [in] what Allah sends down from the sky of provision and gives life thereby to the earth after its lifelessness and [in His] directing of the winds are signs for a people who reason.

# 4479

These are the verses of Allah which We recite to you in truth. Then in what statement after Allah and His verses will they believe?

# 4480

Woe to every sinful liar

# 4481

Who hears the verses of Allah recited to him, then persists arrogantly as if he had not heard them. So give him tidings of a painful punishment.

# 4482

And when he knows anything of Our verses, he takes them in ridicule. Those will have a humiliating punishment.

# 4483

Before them is Hell, and what they had earned will not avail them at all nor what they had taken besides Allah as allies. And they will have a great punishment.

# 4484

This [Qur'an] is guidance. And those who have disbelieved in the verses of their Lord will have a painful punishment of foul nature.

# 4485

It is Allah who subjected to you the sea so that ships may sail upon it by His command and that you may seek of His bounty; and perhaps you will be grateful.

# 4486

And He has subjected to you whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth - all from Him. Indeed in that are signs for a people who give thought.

# 4487

Say, [O Muhammad], to those who have believed that they [should] forgive those who expect not the days of Allah so that He may recompense a people for what they used to earn.

# 4488

Whoever does a good deed - it is for himself; and whoever does evil - it is against the self. Then to your Lord you will be returned.

# 4489

And We did certainly give the Children of Israel the Scripture and judgement and prophethood, and We provided them with good things and preferred them over the worlds.

# 4490

And We gave them clear proofs of the matter [of religion]. And they did not differ except after knowledge had come to them - out of jealous animosity between themselves. Indeed, your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which they used to differ.

# 4491

Then We put you, [O Muhammad], on an ordained way concerning the matter [of religion]; so follow it and do not follow the inclinations of those who do not know.

# 4492

Indeed, they will never avail you against Allah at all. And indeed, the wrongdoers are allies of one another; but Allah is the protector of the righteous.

# 4493

This [Qur'an] is enlightenment for mankind and guidance and mercy for a people who are certain [in faith].

# 4494

Or do those who commit evils think We will make them like those who have believed and done righteous deeds - [make them] equal in their life and their death? Evil is that which they judge.

# 4495

And Allah created the heavens and earth in truth and so that every soul may be recompensed for what it has earned, and they will not be wronged.

# 4496

Have you seen he who has taken as his god his [own] desire, and Allah has sent him astray due to knowledge and has set a seal upon his hearing and his heart and put over his vision a veil? So who will guide him after Allah? Then will you not be reminded?

# 4497

And they say, "There is not but our worldly life; we die and live, and nothing destroys us except time." And they have of that no knowledge; they are only assuming.

# 4498

And when Our verses are recited to them as clear evidences, their argument is only that they say, "Bring [back] our forefathers, if you should be truthful."

# 4499

Say, "Allah causes you to live, then causes you to die; then He will assemble you for the Day of Resurrection, about which there is no doubt, but most of the people do not know."

# 4500

And to Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. And the Day the Hour appears - that Day the falsifiers will lose.

# 4501

And you will see every nation kneeling [from fear]. Every nation will be called to its record [and told], "Today you will be recompensed for what you used to do.

# 4502

This, Our record, speaks about you in truth. Indeed, We were having transcribed whatever you used to do."

# 4503

So as for those who believed and did righteous deeds, their Lord will admit them into His mercy. That is what is the clear attainment.

# 4504

But as for those who disbelieved, [it will be said], "Were not Our verses recited to you, but you were arrogant and became a people of criminals?

# 4505

And when it was said, 'Indeed, the promise of Allah is truth and the Hour [is coming] - no doubt about it,' you said, 'We know not what is the Hour. We assume only assumption, and we are not convinced.' "

# 4506

And the evil consequences of what they did will appear to them, and they will be enveloped by what they used to ridicule.

# 4507

And it will be said, "Today We will forget you as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours, and your refuge is the Fire, and for you there are no helpers.

# 4508

That is because you took the verses of Allah in ridicule, and worldly life deluded you." So that Day they will not be removed from it, nor will they be asked to appease [Allah].

# 4509

Then, to Allah belongs [all] praise - Lord of the heavens and Lord of the earth, Lord of the worlds.

# 4510

And to Him belongs [all] grandeur within the heavens and the earth, and He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 4511

Ha, Meem.

# 4512

The revelation of the Book is from Allah, the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 4513

We did not create the heavens and earth and what is between them except in truth and [for] a specified term. But those who disbelieve, from that of which they are warned, are turning away.

# 4514

Say, [O Muhammad], "Have you considered that which you invoke besides Allah? Show me what they have created of the earth; or did they have partnership in [creation of] the heavens? Bring me a scripture [revealed] before this or a [remaining] trace of knowledge, if you should be truthful."

# 4515

And who is more astray than he who invokes besides Allah those who will not respond to him until the Day of Resurrection, and they, of their invocation, are unaware.

# 4516

And when the people are gathered [that Day], they [who were invoked] will be enemies to them, and they will be deniers of their worship.

# 4517

And when Our verses are recited to them as clear evidences, those who disbelieve say of the truth when it has come to them, "This is obvious magic."

# 4518

Or do they say, "He has invented it?" Say, "If I have invented it, you will not possess for me [the power of protection] from Allah at all. He is most knowing of that in which you are involved. Sufficient is He as Witness between me and you, and He is the Forgiving the Merciful."

# 4519

Say, "I am not something original among the messengers, nor do I know what will be done with me or with you. I only follow that which is revealed to me, and I am not but a clear warner."

# 4520

Say, "Have you considered: if the Qur'an was from Allah, and you disbelieved in it while a witness from the Children of Israel has testified to something similar and believed while you were arrogant...?" Indeed, Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.

# 4521

And those who disbelieve say of those who believe, "If it had [truly] been good, they would not have preceded us to it." And when they are not guided by it, they will say, "This is an ancient falsehood."

# 4522

And before it was the scripture of Moses to lead and as a mercy. And this is a confirming Book in an Arabic tongue to warn those who have wronged and as good tidings to the doers of good.

# 4523

Indeed, those who have said, "Our Lord is Allah," and then remained on a right course - there will be no fear concerning them, nor will they grieve.

# 4524

Those are the companions of Paradise, abiding eternally therein as reward for what they used to do.

# 4525

And We have enjoined upon man, to his parents, good treatment. His mother carried him with hardship and gave birth to him with hardship, and his gestation and weaning [period] is thirty months. [He grows] until, when he reaches maturity and reaches [the age of] forty years, he says, "My Lord, enable me to be grateful for Your favor which You have bestowed upon me and upon my parents and to work righteousness of which You will approve and make righteous for me my offspring. Indeed, I have repented to You, and indeed, I am of the Muslims."

# 4526

Those are the ones from whom We will accept the best of what they did and overlook their misdeeds, [their being] among the companions of Paradise. [That is] the promise of truth which they had been promised.

# 4527

But one who says to his parents, "Uff to you; do you promise me that I will be brought forth [from the earth] when generations before me have already passed on [into oblivion]?" while they call to Allah for help [and to their son], "Woe to you! Believe! Indeed, the promise of Allah is truth." But he says, "This is not but legends of the former people" -

# 4528

Those are the ones upon whom the word has come into effect, [who will be] among nations which had passed on before them of jinn and men. Indeed, they [all] were losers.

# 4529

And for all there are degrees [of reward and punishment] for what they have done, and [it is] so that He may fully compensate them for their deeds, and they will not be wronged.

# 4530

And the Day those who disbelieved are exposed to the Fire [it will be said], "You exhausted your pleasures during your worldly life and enjoyed them, so this Day you will be awarded the punishment of [extreme] humiliation because you were arrogant upon the earth without right and because you were defiantly disobedient."

# 4531

And mention, [O Muhammad], the brother of 'Aad, when he warned his people in the [region of] al-Ahqaf - and warners had already passed on before him and after him - [saying], "Do not worship except Allah. Indeed, I fear for you the punishment of a terrible day."

# 4532

They said, "Have you come to delude us away from our gods? Then bring us what you promise us, if you should be of the truthful."

# 4533

He said, "Knowledge [of its time] is only with Allah, and I convey to you that with which I was sent; but I see you [to be] a people behaving ignorantly."

# 4534

And when they saw it as a cloud approaching their valleys, they said, "This is a cloud bringing us rain!" Rather, it is that for which you were impatient: a wind, within it a painful punishment,

# 4535

Destroying everything by command of its Lord. And they became so that nothing was seen [of them] except their dwellings. Thus do We recompense the criminal people.

# 4536

And We had certainly established them in such as We have not established you, and We made for them hearing and vision and hearts. But their hearing and vision and hearts availed them not from anything [of the punishment] when they were [continually] rejecting the signs of Allah; and they were enveloped by what they used to ridicule.

# 4537

And We have already destroyed what surrounds you of [those] cities, and We have diversified the signs [or verses] that perhaps they might return [from disbelief].

# 4538

Then why did those they took besides Allah as deities by which to approach [Him] not aid them? But they had strayed from them. And that was their falsehood and what they were inventing.

# 4539

And [mention, O Muhammad], when We directed to you a few of the jinn, listening to the Qur'an. And when they attended it, they said, "Listen quietly." And when it was concluded, they went back to their people as warners.

# 4540

They said, "O our people, indeed we have heard a [recited] Book revealed after Moses confirming what was before it which guides to the truth and to a straight path.

# 4541

O our people, respond to the Messenger of Allah and believe in him; Allah will forgive for you your sins and protect you from a painful punishment.

# 4542

But he who does not respond to the Caller of Allah will not cause failure [to Him] upon earth, and he will not have besides Him any protectors. Those are in manifest error."

# 4543

Do they not see that Allah, who created the heavens and earth and did not fail in their creation, is able to give life to the dead? Yes. Indeed, He is over all things competent.

# 4544

And the Day those who disbelieved are exposed to the Fire [it will be said], "Is this not the truth?" They will say, "Yes, by our Lord." He will say, "Then taste the punishment because you used to disbelieve."

# 4545

So be patient, [O Muhammad], as were those of determination among the messengers and do not be impatient for them. It will be - on the Day they see that which they are promised - as though they had not remained [in the world] except an hour of a day. [This is] notification. And will [any] be destroyed except the defiantly disobedient people?

# 4546

Those who disbelieve and avert [people] from the way of Allah - He will waste their deeds.

# 4547

And those who believe and do righteous deeds and believe in what has been sent down upon Muhammad - and it is the truth from their Lord - He will remove from them their misdeeds and amend their condition.

# 4548

That is because those who disbelieve follow falsehood, and those who believe follow the truth from their Lord. Thus does Allah present to the people their comparisons.

# 4549

So when you meet those who disbelieve [in battle], strike [their] necks until, when you have inflicted slaughter upon them, then secure their bonds, and either [confer] favor afterwards or ransom [them] until the war lays down its burdens. That [is the command]. And if Allah had willed, He could have taken vengeance upon them [Himself], but [He ordered armed struggle] to test some of you by means of others. And those who are killed in the cause of Allah - never will He waste their deeds.

# 4550

He will guide them and amend their condition

# 4551

And admit them to Paradise, which He has made known to them.

# 4552

O you who have believed, if you support Allah, He will support you and plant firmly your feet.

# 4553

But those who disbelieve - for them is misery, and He will waste their deeds.

# 4554

That is because they disliked what Allah revealed, so He rendered worthless their deeds.

# 4555

Have they not traveled through the land and seen how was the end of those before them? Allah destroyed [everything] over them, and for the disbelievers is something comparable.

# 4556

That is because Allah is the protector of those who have believed and because the disbelievers have no protector.

# 4557

Indeed, Allah will admit those who have believed and done righteous deeds to gardens beneath which rivers flow, but those who disbelieve enjoy themselves and eat as grazing livestock eat, and the Fire will be a residence for them.

# 4558

And how many a city was stronger than your city [Makkah] which drove you out? We destroyed them; and there was no helper for them.

# 4559

So is he who is on clear evidence from his Lord like him to whom the evil of his work has been made attractive and they follow their [own] desires?

# 4560

Is the description of Paradise, which the righteous are promised, wherein are rivers of water unaltered, rivers of milk the taste of which never changes, rivers of wine delicious to those who drink, and rivers of purified honey, in which they will have from all [kinds of] fruits and forgiveness from their Lord, like [that of] those who abide eternally in the Fire and are given to drink scalding water that will sever their intestines?

# 4561

And among them, [O Muhammad], are those who listen to you, until when they depart from you, they say to those who were given knowledge, "What has he said just now?" Those are the ones of whom Allah has sealed over their hearts and who have followed their [own] desires.

# 4562

And those who are guided - He increases them in guidance and gives them their righteousness.

# 4563

Then do they await except that the Hour should come upon them unexpectedly? But already there have come [some of] its indications. Then what good to them, when it has come, will be their remembrance?

# 4564

So know, [O Muhammad], that there is no deity except Allah and ask forgiveness for your sin and for the believing men and believing women. And Allah knows of your movement and your resting place.

# 4565

Those who believe say, "Why has a surah not been sent down? But when a precise surah is revealed and fighting is mentioned therein, you see those in whose hearts is hypocrisy looking at you with a look of one overcome by death. And more appropriate for them [would have been]

# 4566

Obedience and good words. And when the matter [of fighting] was determined, if they had been true to Allah, it would have been better for them.

# 4567

So would you perhaps, if you turned away, cause corruption on earth and sever your [ties of] relationship?

# 4568

Those [who do so] are the ones that Allah has cursed, so He deafened them and blinded their vision.

# 4569

Then do they not reflect upon the Qur'an, or are there locks upon [their] hearts?

# 4570

Indeed, those who reverted back [to disbelief] after guidance had become clear to them - Satan enticed them and prolonged hope for them.

# 4571

That is because they said to those who disliked what Allah sent down, "We will obey you in part of the matter." And Allah knows what they conceal.

# 4572

Then how [will it be] when the angels take them in death, striking their faces and their backs?

# 4573

That is because they followed what angered Allah and disliked [what earns] His pleasure, so He rendered worthless their deeds.

# 4574

Or do those in whose hearts is disease think that Allah would never expose their [feelings of] hatred?

# 4575

And if We willed, We could show them to you, and you would know them by their mark; but you will surely know them by the tone of [their] speech. And Allah knows your deeds.

# 4576

And We will surely test you until We make evident those who strive among you [for the cause of Allah] and the patient, and We will test your affairs.

# 4577

Indeed, those who disbelieved and averted [people] from the path of Allah and opposed the Messenger after guidance had become clear to them - never will they harm Allah at all, and He will render worthless their deeds.

# 4578

O you who have believed, obey Allah and obey the Messenger and do not invalidate your deeds.

# 4579

Indeed, those who disbelieved and averted [people] from the path of Allah and then died while they were disbelievers - never will Allah forgive them.

# 4580

So do not weaken and call for peace while you are superior; and Allah is with you and will never deprive you of [the reward of] your deeds.

# 4581

[This] worldly life is only amusement and diversion. And if you believe and fear Allah, He will give you your rewards and not ask you for your properties.

# 4582

If He should ask you for them and press you, you would withhold, and He would expose your unwillingness.

# 4583

Here you are - those invited to spend in the cause of Allah - but among you are those who withhold [out of greed]. And whoever withholds only withholds [benefit] from himself; and Allah is the Free of need, while you are the needy. And if you turn away, He will replace you with another people; then they will not be the likes of you.

# 4584

Indeed, We have given you, [O Muhammad], a clear conquest

# 4585

That Allah may forgive for you what preceded of your sin and what will follow and complete His favor upon you and guide you to a straight path

# 4586

And [that] Allah may aid you with a mighty victory.

# 4587

It is He who sent down tranquillity into the hearts of the believers that they would increase in faith along with their [present] faith. And to Allah belong the soldiers of the heavens and the earth, and ever is Allah Knowing and Wise.

# 4588

[And] that He may admit the believing men and the believing women to gardens beneath which rivers flow to abide therein eternally and remove from them their misdeeds - and ever is that, in the sight of Allah, a great attainment -

# 4589

And [that] He may punish the hypocrite men and hypocrite women, and the polytheist men and polytheist women - those who assume about Allah an assumption of evil nature. Upon them is a misfortune of evil nature; and Allah has become angry with them and has cursed them and prepared for them Hell, and evil it is as a destination.

# 4590

And to Allah belong the soldiers of the heavens and the earth. And ever is Allah Exalted in Might and Wise.

# 4591

Indeed, We have sent you as a witness and a bringer of good tidings and a warner

# 4592

That you [people] may believe in Allah and His Messenger and honor him and respect the Prophet and exalt Allah morning and afternoon.

# 4593

Indeed, those who pledge allegiance to you, [O Muhammad] - they are actually pledging allegiance to Allah. The hand of Allah is over their hands. So he who breaks his word only breaks it to the detriment of himself. And he who fulfills that which he has promised Allah - He will give him a great reward.

# 4594

Those who remained behind of the bedouins will say to you, "Our properties and our families occupied us, so ask forgiveness for us." They say with their tongues what is not within their hearts. Say, "Then who could prevent Allah at all if He intended for you harm or intended for you benefit? Rather, ever is Allah, with what you do, Acquainted.

# 4595

But you thought that the Messenger and the believers would never return to their families, ever, and that was made pleasing in your hearts. And you assumed an assumption of evil and became a people ruined."

# 4596

And whoever has not believed in Allah and His Messenger - then indeed, We have prepared for the disbelievers a Blaze.

# 4597

And to Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He forgives whom He wills and punishes whom He wills. And ever is Allah Forgiving and Merciful.

# 4598

Those who remained behind will say when you set out toward the war booty to take it, "Let us follow you." They wish to change the words of Allah. Say, "Never will you follow us. Thus did Allah say before." So they will say, "Rather, you envy us." But [in fact] they were not understanding except a little.

# 4599

Say to those who remained behind of the bedouins, "You will be called to [face] a people of great military might; you may fight them, or they will submit. So if you obey, Allah will give you a good reward; but if you turn away as you turned away before, He will punish you with a painful punishment."

# 4600

There is not upon the blind any guilt or upon the lame any guilt or upon the ill any guilt [for remaining behind]. And whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger - He will admit him to gardens beneath which rivers flow; but whoever turns away - He will punish him with a painful punishment.

# 4601

Certainly was Allah pleased with the believers when they pledged allegiance to you, [O Muhammad], under the tree, and He knew what was in their hearts, so He sent down tranquillity upon them and rewarded them with an imminent conquest

# 4602

And much war booty which they will take. And ever is Allah Exalted in Might and Wise.

# 4603

Allah has promised you much booty that you will take [in the future] and has hastened for you this [victory] and withheld the hands of people from you - that it may be a sign for the believers and [that] He may guide you to a straight path.

# 4604

And [He promises] other [victories] that you were [so far] unable to [realize] which Allah has already encompassed. And ever is Allah, over all things, competent.

# 4605

And if those [Makkans] who disbelieve had fought you, they would have turned their backs [in flight]. Then they would not find a protector or a helper.

# 4606

[This is] the established way of Allah which has occurred before. And never will you find in the way of Allah any change.

# 4607

And it is He who withheld their hands from you and your hands from them within [the area of] Makkah after He caused you to overcome them. And ever is Allah of what you do, Seeing.

# 4608

They are the ones who disbelieved and obstructed you from al-Masjid al-Haram while the offering was prevented from reaching its place of sacrifice. And if not for believing men and believing women whom you did not know - that you might trample them and there would befall you because of them dishonor without [your] knowledge - [you would have been permitted to enter Makkah]. [This was so] that Allah might admit to His mercy whom He willed. If they had been apart [from them], We would have punished those who disbelieved among them with painful punishment

# 4609

When those who disbelieved had put into their hearts chauvinism - the chauvinism of the time of ignorance. But Allah sent down His tranquillity upon His Messenger and upon the believers and imposed upon them the word of righteousness, and they were more deserving of it and worthy of it. And ever is Allah, of all things, Knowing.

# 4610

Certainly has Allah showed to His Messenger the vision in truth. You will surely enter al-Masjid al-Haram, if Allah wills, in safety, with your heads shaved and [hair] shortened, not fearing [anyone]. He knew what you did not know and has arranged before that a conquest near [at hand].

# 4611

It is He who sent His Messenger with guidance and the religion of truth to manifest it over all religion. And sufficient is Allah as Witness.

# 4612

Muhammad is the Messenger of Allah; and those with him are forceful against the disbelievers, merciful among themselves. You see them bowing and prostrating [in prayer], seeking bounty from Allah and [His] pleasure. Their mark is on their faces from the trace of prostration. That is their description in the Torah. And their description in the Gospel is as a plant which produces its offshoots and strengthens them so they grow firm and stand upon their stalks, delighting the sowers - so that Allah may enrage by them the disbelievers. Allah has promised those who believe and do righteous deeds among them forgiveness and a great reward.

# 4613

O you who have believed, do not put [yourselves] before Allah and His Messenger but fear Allah. Indeed, Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

# 4614

O you who have believed, do not raise your voices above the voice of the Prophet or be loud to him in speech like the loudness of some of you to others, lest your deeds become worthless while you perceive not.

# 4615

Indeed, those who lower their voices before the Messenger of Allah - they are the ones whose hearts Allah has tested for righteousness. For them is forgiveness and great reward.

# 4616

Indeed, those who call you, [O Muhammad], from behind the chambers - most of them do not use reason.

# 4617

And if they had been patient until you [could] come out to them, it would have been better for them. But Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 4618

O you who have believed, if there comes to you a disobedient one with information, investigate, lest you harm a people out of ignorance and become, over what you have done, regretful.

# 4619

And know that among you is the Messenger of Allah. If he were to obey you in much of the matter, you would be in difficulty, but Allah has endeared to you the faith and has made it pleasing in your hearts and has made hateful to you disbelief, defiance and disobedience. Those are the [rightly] guided.

# 4620

[It is] as bounty from Allah and favor. And Allah is Knowing and Wise.

# 4621

And if two factions among the believers should fight, then make settlement between the two. But if one of them oppresses the other, then fight against the one that oppresses until it returns to the ordinance of Allah. And if it returns, then make settlement between them in justice and act justly. Indeed, Allah loves those who act justly.

# 4622

The believers are but brothers, so make settlement between your brothers. And fear Allah that you may receive mercy.

# 4623

O you who have believed, let not a people ridicule [another] people; perhaps they may be better than them; nor let women ridicule [other] women; perhaps they may be better than them. And do not insult one another and do not call each other by [offensive] nicknames. Wretched is the name of disobedience after [one's] faith. And whoever does not repent - then it is those who are the wrongdoers.

# 4624

O you who have believed, avoid much [negative] assumption. Indeed, some assumption is sin. And do not spy or backbite each other. Would one of you like to eat the flesh of his brother when dead? You would detest it. And fear Allah; indeed, Allah is Accepting of repentance and Merciful.

# 4625

O mankind, indeed We have created you from male and female and made you peoples and tribes that you may know one another. Indeed, the most noble of you in the sight of Allah is the most righteous of you. Indeed, Allah is Knowing and Acquainted.

# 4626

The bedouins say, "We have believed." Say, "You have not [yet] believed; but say [instead], 'We have submitted,' for faith has not yet entered your hearts. And if you obey Allah and His Messenger, He will not deprive you from your deeds of anything. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful."

# 4627

The believers are only the ones who have believed in Allah and His Messenger and then doubt not but strive with their properties and their lives in the cause of Allah. It is those who are the truthful.

# 4628

Say, "Would you acquaint Allah with your religion while Allah knows whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth, and Allah is Knowing of all things?"

# 4629

They consider it a favor to you that they have accepted Islam. Say, "Do not consider your Islam a favor to me. Rather, Allah has conferred favor upon you that He has guided you to the faith, if you should be truthful."

# 4630

Indeed, Allah knows the unseen [aspects] of the heavens and the earth. And Allah is Seeing of what you do.

# 4631

Qaf. By the honored Qur'an...

# 4632

But they wonder that there has come to them a warner from among themselves, and the disbelievers say, "This is an amazing thing.

# 4633

When we have died and have become dust, [we will return to life]? That is a distant return."

# 4634

We know what the earth diminishes of them, and with Us is a retaining record.

# 4635

But they denied the truth when it came to them, so they are in a confused condition.

# 4636

Have they not looked at the heaven above them - how We structured it and adorned it and [how] it has no rifts?

# 4637

And the earth - We spread it out and cast therein firmly set mountains and made grow therein [something] of every beautiful kind,

# 4638

Giving insight and a reminder for every servant who turns [to Allah].

# 4639

And We have sent down blessed rain from the sky and made grow thereby gardens and grain from the harvest

# 4640

And lofty palm trees having fruit arranged in layers -

# 4641

As provision for the servants, and We have given life thereby to a dead land. Thus is the resurrection.

# 4642

The people of Noah denied before them, and the companions of the well and Thamud

# 4643

And 'Aad and Pharaoh and the brothers of Lot

# 4644

And the companions of the thicket and the people of Tubba'. All denied the messengers, so My threat was justly fulfilled.

# 4645

Did We fail in the first creation? But they are in confusion over a new creation.

# 4646

And We have already created man and know what his soul whispers to him, and We are closer to him than [his] jugular vein

# 4647

When the two receivers receive, seated on the right and on the left.

# 4648

Man does not utter any word except that with him is an observer prepared [to record].

# 4649

And the intoxication of death will bring the truth; that is what you were trying to avoid.

# 4650

And the Horn will be blown. That is the Day of [carrying out] the threat.

# 4651

And every soul will come, with it a driver and a witness.

# 4652

[It will be said], "You were certainly in unmindfulness of this, and We have removed from you your cover, so your sight, this Day, is sharp."

# 4653

And his companion, [the angel], will say, "This [record] is what is with me, prepared."

# 4654

[Allah will say], "Throw into Hell every obstinate disbeliever,

# 4655

Preventer of good, aggressor, and doubter,

# 4656

Who made [as equal] with Allah another deity; then throw him into the severe punishment."

# 4657

His [devil] companion will say, "Our Lord, I did not make him transgress, but he [himself] was in extreme error."

# 4658

[Allah] will say, "Do not dispute before Me, while I had already presented to you the warning.

# 4659

The word will not be changed with Me, and never will I be unjust to the servants."

# 4660

On the Day We will say to Hell, "Have you been filled?" and it will say, "Are there some more,"

# 4661

And Paradise will be brought near to the righteous, not far,

# 4662

[It will be said], "This is what you were promised - for every returner [to Allah] and keeper [of His covenant]

# 4663

Who feared the Most Merciful unseen and came with a heart returning [in repentance].

# 4664

Enter it in peace. This is the Day of Eternity."

# 4665

They will have whatever they wish therein, and with Us is more.

# 4666

And how many a generation before them did We destroy who were greater than them in [striking] power and had explored throughout the lands. Is there any place of escape?

# 4667

Indeed in that is a reminder for whoever has a heart or who listens while he is present [in mind].

# 4668

And We did certainly create the heavens and earth and what is between them in six days, and there touched Us no weariness.

# 4669

So be patient, [O Muhammad], over what they say and exalt [Allah] with praise of your Lord before the rising of the sun and before its setting,

# 4670

And [in part] of the night exalt Him and after prostration.

# 4671

And listen on the Day when the Caller will call out from a place that is near -

# 4672

The Day they will hear the blast [of the Horn] in truth. That is the Day of Emergence [from the graves].

# 4673

Indeed, it is We who give life and cause death, and to Us is the destination

# 4674

On the Day the earth breaks away from them [and they emerge] rapidly; that is a gathering easy for Us.

# 4675

We are most knowing of what they say, and you are not over them a tyrant. But remind by the Qur'an whoever fears My threat.

# 4676

By those [winds] scattering [dust] dispersing

# 4677

And those [clouds] carrying a load [of water]

# 4678

And those [ships] sailing with ease

# 4679

And those [angels] apportioning [each] matter,

# 4680

Indeed, what you are promised is true.

# 4681

And indeed, the recompense is to occur.

# 4682

By the heaven containing pathways,

# 4683

Indeed, you are in differing speech.

# 4684

Deluded away from the Qur'an is he who is deluded.

# 4685

Destroyed are the falsifiers

# 4686

Who are within a flood [of confusion] and heedless.

# 4687

They ask, "When is the Day of Recompense?"

# 4688

[It is] the Day they will be tormented over the Fire

# 4689

[And will be told], "Taste your torment. This is that for which you were impatient."

# 4690

Indeed, the righteous will be among gardens and springs,

# 4691

Accepting what their Lord has given them. Indeed, they were before that doers of good.

# 4692

They used to sleep but little of the night,

# 4693

And in the hours before dawn they would ask forgiveness,

# 4694

And from their properties was [given] the right of the [needy] petitioner and the deprived.

# 4695

And on the earth are signs for the certain [in faith]

# 4696

And in yourselves. Then will you not see?

# 4697

And in the heaven is your provision and whatever you are promised.

# 4698

Then by the Lord of the heaven and earth, indeed, it is truth - just as [sure as] it is that you are speaking.

# 4699

Has there reached you the story of the honored guests of Abraham? -

# 4700

When they entered upon him and said, "[We greet you with] peace." He answered, "[And upon you] peace, [you are] a people unknown.

# 4701

Then he went to his family and came with a fat [roasted] calf

# 4702

And placed it near them; he said, "Will you not eat?"

# 4703

And he felt from them apprehension. They said, "Fear not," and gave him good tidings of a learned boy.

# 4704

And his wife approached with a cry [of alarm] and struck her face and said, "[I am] a barren old woman!"

# 4705

They said, "Thus has said your Lord; indeed, He is the Wise, the Knowing."

# 4706

[Abraham] said, "Then what is your business [here], O messengers?"

# 4707

They said, "Indeed, we have been sent to a people of criminals

# 4708

To send down upon them stones of clay,

# 4709

Marked in the presence of your Lord for the transgressors."

# 4710

So We brought out whoever was in the cities of the believers.

# 4711

And We found not within them other than a [single] house of Muslims.

# 4712

And We left therein a sign for those who fear the painful punishment.

# 4713

And in Moses [was a sign], when We sent him to Pharaoh with clear authority.

# 4714

But he turned away with his supporters and said," A magician or a madman."

# 4715

So We took him and his soldiers and cast them into the sea, and he was blameworthy.

# 4716

And in 'Aad [was a sign], when We sent against them the barren wind.

# 4717

It left nothing of what it came upon but that it made it like disintegrated ruins.

# 4718

And in Thamud, when it was said to them, "Enjoy yourselves for a time."

# 4719

But they were insolent toward the command of their Lord, so the thunderbolt seized them while they were looking on.

# 4720

And they were unable to arise, nor could they defend themselves.

# 4721

And [We destroyed] the people of Noah before; indeed, they were a people defiantly disobedient.

# 4722

And the heaven We constructed with strength, and indeed, We are [its] expander.

# 4723

And the earth We have spread out, and excellent is the preparer.

# 4724

And of all things We created two mates; perhaps you will remember.

# 4725

So flee to Allah. Indeed, I am to you from Him a clear warner.

# 4726

And do not make [as equal] with Allah another deity. Indeed, I am to you from Him a clear warner.

# 4727

Similarly, there came not to those before them any messenger except that they said, "A magician or a madman."

# 4728

Did they suggest it to them? Rather, they [themselves] are a transgressing people.

# 4729

So leave them, [O Muhammad], for you are not to be blamed.

# 4730

And remind, for indeed, the reminder benefits the believers.

# 4731

And I did not create the jinn and mankind except to worship Me.

# 4732

I do not want from them any provision, nor do I want them to feed Me.

# 4733

Indeed, it is Allah who is the [continual] Provider, the firm possessor of strength.

# 4734

And indeed, for those who have wronged is a portion [of punishment] like the portion of their predecessors, so let them not impatiently urge Me.

# 4735

And woe to those who have disbelieved from their Day which they are promised.

# 4736

By the mount

# 4737

And [by] a Book inscribed

# 4738

In parchment spread open

# 4739

And [by] the frequented House

# 4740

And [by] the heaven raised high

# 4741

And [by] the sea filled [with fire],

# 4742

Indeed, the punishment of your Lord will occur.

# 4743

Of it there is no preventer.

# 4744

On the Day the heaven will sway with circular motion

# 4745

And the mountains will pass on, departing -

# 4746

Then woe, that Day, to the deniers,

# 4747

Who are in [empty] discourse amusing themselves.

# 4748

The Day they are thrust toward the fire of Hell with a [violent] thrust, [its angels will say],

# 4749

"This is the Fire which you used to deny.

# 4750

Then is this magic, or do you not see?

# 4751

[Enter to] burn therein; then be patient or impatient - it is all the same for you. You are only being recompensed [for] what you used to do."

# 4752

Indeed, the righteous will be in gardens and pleasure,

# 4753

Enjoying what their Lord has given them, and their Lord protected them from the punishment of Hellfire.

# 4754

[They will be told], "Eat and drink in satisfaction for what you used to do."

# 4755

They will be reclining on thrones lined up, and We will marry them to fair women with large, [beautiful] eyes.

# 4756

And those who believed and whose descendants followed them in faith - We will join with them their descendants, and We will not deprive them of anything of their deeds. Every person, for what he earned, is retained.

# 4757

And We will provide them with fruit and meat from whatever they desire.

# 4758

They will exchange with one another a cup [of wine] wherein [results] no ill speech or commission of sin.

# 4759

There will circulate among them [servant] boys [especially] for them, as if they were pearls well-protected.

# 4760

And they will approach one another, inquiring of each other.

# 4761

They will say, "Indeed, we were previously among our people fearful [of displeasing Allah].

# 4762

So Allah conferred favor upon us and protected us from the punishment of the Scorching Fire.

# 4763

Indeed, we used to supplicate Him before. Indeed, it is He who is the Beneficent, the Merciful."

# 4764

So remind [O Muhammad], for you are not, by the favor of your Lord, a soothsayer or a madman.

# 4765

Or do they say [of you], "A poet for whom we await a misfortune of time?"

# 4766

Say, "Wait, for indeed I am, with you, among the waiters."

# 4767

Or do their minds command them to [say] this, or are they a transgressing people?

# 4768

Or do they say, "He has made it up"? Rather, they do not believe.

# 4769

Then let them produce a statement like it, if they should be truthful.

# 4770

Or were they created by nothing, or were they the creators [of themselves]?

# 4771

Or did they create the heavens and the earth? Rather, they are not certain.

# 4772

Or have they the depositories [containing the provision] of your Lord? Or are they the controllers [of them]?

# 4773

Or have they a stairway [into the heaven] upon which they listen? Then let their listener produce a clear authority.

# 4774

Or has He daughters while you have sons?

# 4775

Or do you, [O Muhammad], ask of them a payment, so they are by debt burdened down?

# 4776

Or have they [knowledge of] the unseen, so they write [it] down?

# 4777

Or do they intend a plan? But those who disbelieve - they are the object of a plan.

# 4778

Or have they a deity other than Allah? Exalted is Allah above whatever they associate with Him.

# 4779

And if they were to see a fragment from the sky falling, they would say, "[It is merely] clouds heaped up."

# 4780

So leave them until they meet their Day in which they will be struck insensible -

# 4781

The Day their plan will not avail them at all, nor will they be helped.

# 4782

And indeed, for those who have wronged is a punishment before that, but most of them do not know.

# 4783

And be patient, [O Muhammad], for the decision of your Lord, for indeed, you are in Our eyes. And exalt [Allah] with praise of your Lord when you arise.

# 4784

And in a part of the night exalt Him and after [the setting of] the stars.

# 4785

By the star when it descends,

# 4786

Your companion [Muhammad] has not strayed, nor has he erred,

# 4787

Nor does he speak from [his own] inclination.

# 4788

It is not but a revelation revealed,

# 4789

Taught to him by one intense in strength -

# 4790

One of soundness. And he rose to [his] true form

# 4791

While he was in the higher [part of the] horizon.

# 4792

Then he approached and descended

# 4793

And was at a distance of two bow lengths or nearer.

# 4794

And he revealed to His Servant what he revealed.

# 4795

The heart did not lie [about] what it saw.

# 4796

So will you dispute with him over what he saw?

# 4797

And he certainly saw him in another descent

# 4798

At the Lote Tree of the Utmost Boundary -

# 4799

Near it is the Garden of Refuge -

# 4800

When there covered the Lote Tree that which covered [it].

# 4801

The sight [of the Prophet] did not swerve, nor did it transgress [its limit].

# 4802

He certainly saw of the greatest signs of his Lord.

# 4803

So have you considered al-Lat and al-'Uzza?

# 4804

And Manat, the third - the other one?

# 4805

Is the male for you and for Him the female?

# 4806

That, then, is an unjust division.

# 4807

They are not but [mere] names you have named them - you and your forefathers - for which Allah has sent down no authority. They follow not except assumption and what [their] souls desire, and there has already come to them from their Lord guidance.

# 4808

Or is there for man whatever he wishes?

# 4809

Rather, to Allah belongs the Hereafter and the first [life].

# 4810

And how many angels there are in the heavens whose intercession will not avail at all except [only] after Allah has permitted [it] to whom He wills and approves.

# 4811

Indeed, those who do not believe in the Hereafter name the angels female names,

# 4812

And they have thereof no knowledge. They follow not except assumption, and indeed, assumption avails not against the truth at all.

# 4813

So turn away from whoever turns his back on Our message and desires not except the worldly life.

# 4814

That is their sum of knowledge. Indeed, your Lord is most knowing of who strays from His way, and He is most knowing of who is guided.

# 4815

And to Allah belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth - that He may recompense those who do evil with [the penalty of] what they have done and recompense those who do good with the best [reward] -

# 4816

Those who avoid the major sins and immoralities, only [committing] slight ones. Indeed, your Lord is vast in forgiveness. He was most knowing of you when He produced you from the earth and when you were fetuses in the wombs of your mothers. So do not claim yourselves to be pure; He is most knowing of who fears Him.

# 4817

Have you seen the one who turned away

# 4818

And gave a little and [then] refrained?

# 4819

Does he have knowledge of the unseen, so he sees?

# 4820

Or has he not been informed of what was in the scriptures of Moses

# 4821

And [of] Abraham, who fulfilled [his obligations] -

# 4822

That no bearer of burdens will bear the burden of another

# 4823

And that there is not for man except that [good] for which he strives

# 4824

And that his effort is going to be seen -

# 4825

Then he will be recompensed for it with the fullest recompense

# 4826

And that to your Lord is the finality

# 4827

And that it is He who makes [one] laugh and weep

# 4828

And that it is He who causes death and gives life

# 4829

And that He creates the two mates - the male and female -

# 4830

From a sperm-drop when it is emitted

# 4831

And that [incumbent] upon Him is the next creation

# 4832

And that it is He who enriches and suffices

# 4833

And that it is He who is the Lord of Sirius

# 4834

And that He destroyed the first [people of] 'Aad

# 4835

And Thamud - and He did not spare [them] -

# 4836

And the people of Noah before. Indeed, it was they who were [even] more unjust and oppressing.

# 4837

And the overturned towns He hurled down

# 4838

And covered them by that which He covered.

# 4839

Then which of the favors of your Lord do you doubt?

# 4840

This [Prophet] is a warner like the former warners.

# 4841

The Approaching Day has approached.

# 4842

Of it, [from those] besides Allah, there is no remover.

# 4843

Then at this statement do you wonder?

# 4844

And you laugh and do not weep

# 4845

While you are proudly sporting?

# 4846

So prostrate to Allah and worship [Him].

# 4847

The Hour has come near, and the moon has split [in two].

# 4848

And if they see a miracle, they turn away and say, "Passing magic."

# 4849

And they denied and followed their inclinations. But for every matter is a [time of] settlement.

# 4850

And there has already come to them of information that in which there is deterrence -

# 4851

Extensive wisdom - but warning does not avail [them].

# 4852

So leave them, [O Muhammad]. The Day the Caller calls to something forbidding,

# 4853

Their eyes humbled, they will emerge from the graves as if they were locusts spreading,

# 4854

Racing ahead toward the Caller. The disbelievers will say, "This is a difficult Day."

# 4855

The people of Noah denied before them, and they denied Our servant and said, "A madman," and he was repelled.

# 4856

So he invoked his Lord, "Indeed, I am overpowered, so help."

# 4857

Then We opened the gates of the heaven with rain pouring down

# 4858

And caused the earth to burst with springs, and the waters met for a matter already predestined.

# 4859

And We carried him on a [construction of] planks and nails,

# 4860

Sailing under Our observation as reward for he who had been denied.

# 4861

And We left it as a sign, so is there any who will remember?

# 4862

And how [severe] were My punishment and warning.

# 4863

And We have certainly made the Qur'an easy for remembrance, so is there any who will remember?

# 4864

'Aad denied; and how [severe] were My punishment and warning.

# 4865

Indeed, We sent upon them a screaming wind on a day of continuous misfortune,

# 4866

Extracting the people as if they were trunks of palm trees uprooted.

# 4867

And how [severe] were My punishment and warning.

# 4868

And We have certainly made the Qur'an easy for remembrance, so is there any who will remember?

# 4869

Thamud denied the warning

# 4870

And said, "Is it one human being among us that we should follow? Indeed, we would then be in error and madness.

# 4871

Has the message been sent down upon him from among us? Rather, he is an insolent liar."

# 4872

They will know tomorrow who is the insolent liar.

# 4873

Indeed, We are sending the she-camel as trial for them, so watch them and be patient.

# 4874

And inform them that the water is shared between them, each [day of] drink attended [by turn].

# 4875

But they called their companion, and he dared and hamstrung [her].

# 4876

And how [severe] were My punishment and warning.

# 4877

Indeed, We sent upon them one blast from the sky, and they became like the dry twig fragments of an [animal] pen.

# 4878

And We have certainly made the Qur'an easy for remembrance, so is there any who will remember?

# 4879

The people of Lot denied the warning.

# 4880

Indeed, We sent upon them a storm of stones, except the family of Lot - We saved them before dawn

# 4881

As favor from us. Thus do We reward he who is grateful.

# 4882

And he had already warned them of Our assault, but they disputed the warning.

# 4883

And they had demanded from him his guests, but We obliterated their eyes, [saying], "Taste My punishment and warning."

# 4884

And there came upon them by morning an abiding punishment.

# 4885

So taste My punishment and warning.

# 4886

And We have certainly made the Qur'an easy for remembrance, so is there any who will remember?

# 4887

And there certainly came to the people of Pharaoh warning.

# 4888

They denied Our signs, all of them, so We seized them with a seizure of one Exalted in Might and Perfect in Ability.

# 4889

Are your disbelievers better than those [former ones], or have you immunity in the scripture?

# 4890

Or do they say, "We are an assembly supporting [each other]"?

# 4891

[Their] assembly will be defeated, and they will turn their backs [in retreat].

# 4892

But the Hour is their appointment [for due punishment], and the Hour is more disastrous and more bitter.

# 4893

Indeed, the criminals are in error and madness.

# 4894

The Day they are dragged into the Fire on their faces [it will be said], "Taste the touch of Saqar."

# 4895

Indeed, all things We created with predestination.

# 4896

And Our command is but one, like a glance of the eye.

# 4897

And We have already destroyed your kinds, so is there any who will remember?

# 4898

And everything they did is in written records.

# 4899

And every small and great [thing] is inscribed.

# 4900

Indeed, the righteous will be among gardens and rivers,

# 4901

In a seat of honor near a Sovereign, Perfect in Ability.

# 4902

The Most Merciful

# 4903

Taught the Qur'an,

# 4904

Created man,

# 4905

[And] taught him eloquence.

# 4906

The sun and the moon [move] by precise calculation,

# 4907

And the stars and trees prostrate.

# 4908

And the heaven He raised and imposed the balance

# 4909

That you not transgress within the balance.

# 4910

And establish weight in justice and do not make deficient the balance.

# 4911

And the earth He laid [out] for the creatures.

# 4912

Therein is fruit and palm trees having sheaths [of dates]

# 4913

And grain having husks and scented plants.

# 4914

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4915

He created man from clay like [that of] pottery.

# 4916

And He created the jinn from a smokeless flame of fire.

# 4917

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4918

[He is] Lord of the two sunrises and Lord of the two sunsets.

# 4919

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4920

He released the two seas, meeting [side by side];

# 4921

Between them is a barrier [so] neither of them transgresses.

# 4922

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4923

From both of them emerge pearl and coral.

# 4924

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4925

And to Him belong the ships [with sails] elevated in the sea like mountains.

# 4926

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4927

Everyone upon the earth will perish,

# 4928

And there will remain the Face of your Lord, Owner of Majesty and Honor.

# 4929

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4930

Whoever is within the heavens and earth asks Him; every day He is bringing about a matter.

# 4931

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4932

We will attend to you, O prominent beings.

# 4933

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4934

O company of jinn and mankind, if you are able to pass beyond the regions of the heavens and the earth, then pass. You will not pass except by authority [from Allah].

# 4935

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4936

There will be sent upon you a flame of fire and smoke, and you will not defend yourselves.

# 4937

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4938

And when the heaven is split open and becomes rose-colored like oil -

# 4939

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4940

Then on that Day none will be asked about his sin among men or jinn.

# 4941

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4942

The criminals will be known by their marks, and they will be seized by the forelocks and the feet.

# 4943

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4944

This is Hell, which the criminals deny.

# 4945

They will go around between it and scalding water, heated [to the utmost degree].

# 4946

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4947

But for he who has feared the position of his Lord are two gardens -

# 4948

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4949

Having [spreading] branches.

# 4950

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4951

In both of them are two springs, flowing.

# 4952

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4953

In both of them are of every fruit, two kinds.

# 4954

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4955

[They are] reclining on beds whose linings are of silk brocade, and the fruit of the two gardens is hanging low.

# 4956

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4957

In them are women limiting [their] glances, untouched before them by man or jinni -

# 4958

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4959

As if they were rubies and coral.

# 4960

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4961

Is the reward for good [anything] but good?

# 4962

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4963

And below them both [in excellence] are two [other] gardens -

# 4964

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4965

Dark green [in color].

# 4966

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4967

In both of them are two springs, spouting.

# 4968

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4969

In both of them are fruit and palm trees and pomegranates.

# 4970

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4971

In them are good and beautiful women -

# 4972

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4973

Fair ones reserved in pavilions -

# 4974

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4975

Untouched before them by man or jinni -

# 4976

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny? -

# 4977

Reclining on green cushions and beautiful fine carpets.

# 4978

So which of the favors of your Lord would you deny?

# 4979

Blessed is the name of your Lord, Owner of Majesty and Honor.

# 4980

When the Occurrence occurs,

# 4981

There is, at its occurrence, no denial.

# 4982

It will bring down [some] and raise up [others].

# 4983

When the earth is shaken with convulsion

# 4984

And the mountains are broken down, crumbling

# 4985

And become dust dispersing.

# 4986

And you become [of] three kinds:

# 4987

Then the companions of the right - what are the companions of the right?

# 4988

And the companions of the left - what are the companions of the left?

# 4989

And the forerunners, the forerunners -

# 4990

Those are the ones brought near [to Allah]

# 4991

In the Gardens of Pleasure,

# 4992

A [large] company of the former peoples

# 4993

And a few of the later peoples,

# 4994

On thrones woven [with ornament],

# 4995

Reclining on them, facing each other.

# 4996

There will circulate among them young boys made eternal

# 4997

With vessels, pitchers and a cup [of wine] from a flowing spring -

# 4998

No headache will they have therefrom, nor will they be intoxicated -

# 4999

And fruit of what they select

# 5000

And the meat of fowl, from whatever they desire.

# 5001

And [for them are] fair women with large, [beautiful] eyes,

# 5002

The likenesses of pearls well-protected,

# 5003

As reward for what they used to do.

# 5004

They will not hear therein ill speech or commission of sin -

# 5005

Only a saying: "Peace, peace."

# 5006

The companions of the right - what are the companions of the right?

# 5007

[They will be] among lote trees with thorns removed

# 5008

And [banana] trees layered [with fruit]

# 5009

And shade extended

# 5010

And water poured out

# 5011

And fruit, abundant [and varied],

# 5012

Neither limited [to season] nor forbidden,

# 5013

And [upon] beds raised high.

# 5014

Indeed, We have produced the women of Paradise in a [new] creation

# 5015

And made them virgins,

# 5016

Devoted [to their husbands] and of equal age,

# 5017

For the companions of the right [who are]

# 5018

A company of the former peoples

# 5019

And a company of the later peoples.

# 5020

And the companions of the left - what are the companions of the left?

# 5021

[They will be] in scorching fire and scalding water

# 5022

And a shade of black smoke,

# 5023

Neither cool nor beneficial.

# 5024

Indeed they were, before that, indulging in affluence,

# 5025

And they used to persist in the great violation,

# 5026

And they used to say, "When we die and become dust and bones, are we indeed to be resurrected?

# 5027

And our forefathers [as well]?"

# 5028

Say, [O Muhammad], "Indeed, the former and the later peoples

# 5029

Are to be gathered together for the appointment of a known Day."

# 5030

Then indeed you, O those astray [who are] deniers,

# 5031

Will be eating from trees of zaqqum

# 5032

And filling with it your bellies

# 5033

And drinking on top of it from scalding water

# 5034

And will drink as the drinking of thirsty camels.

# 5035

That is their accommodation on the Day of Recompense.

# 5036

We have created you, so why do you not believe?

# 5037

Have you seen that which you emit?

# 5038

Is it you who creates it, or are We the Creator?

# 5039

We have decreed death among you, and We are not to be outdone

# 5040

In that We will change your likenesses and produce you in that [form] which you do not know.

# 5041

And you have already known the first creation, so will you not remember?

# 5042

And have you seen that [seed] which you sow?

# 5043

Is it you who makes it grow, or are We the grower?

# 5044

If We willed, We could make it [dry] debris, and you would remain in wonder,

# 5045

[Saying], "Indeed, we are [now] in debt;

# 5046

Rather, we have been deprived."

# 5047

And have you seen the water that you drink?

# 5048

Is it you who brought it down from the clouds, or is it We who bring it down?

# 5049

If We willed, We could make it bitter, so why are you not grateful?

# 5050

And have you seen the fire that you ignite?

# 5051

Is it you who produced its tree, or are We the producer?

# 5052

We have made it a reminder and provision for the travelers,

# 5053

So exalt the name of your Lord, the Most Great.

# 5054

Then I swear by the setting of the stars,

# 5055

And indeed, it is an oath - if you could know - [most] great.

# 5056

Indeed, it is a noble Qur'an

# 5057

In a Register well-protected;

# 5058

None touch it except the purified.

# 5059

[It is] a revelation from the Lord of the worlds.

# 5060

Then is it to this statement that you are indifferent

# 5061

And make [the thanks for] your provision that you deny [the Provider]?

# 5062

Then why, when the soul at death reaches the throat

# 5063

And you are at that time looking on -

# 5064

And Our angels are nearer to him than you, but you do not see -

# 5065

Then why do you not, if you are not to be recompensed,

# 5066

Bring it back, if you should be truthful?

# 5067

And if the deceased was of those brought near to Allah,

# 5068

Then [for him is] rest and bounty and a garden of pleasure.

# 5069

And if he was of the companions of the right,

# 5070

Then [the angels will say], "Peace for you; [you are] from the companions of the right."

# 5071

But if he was of the deniers [who were] astray,

# 5072

Then [for him is] accommodation of scalding water

# 5073

And burning in Hellfire

# 5074

Indeed, this is the true certainty,

# 5075

So exalt the name of your Lord, the Most Great.

# 5076

Whatever is in the heavens and earth exalts Allah, and He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5077

His is the dominion of the heavens and earth. He gives life and causes death, and He is over all things competent.

# 5078

He is the First and the Last, the Ascendant and the Intimate, and He is, of all things, Knowing.

# 5079

It is He who created the heavens and earth in six days and then established Himself above the Throne. He knows what penetrates into the earth and what emerges from it and what descends from the heaven and what ascends therein; and He is with you wherever you are. And Allah, of what you do, is Seeing.

# 5080

His is the dominion of the heavens and earth. And to Allah are returned [all] matters.

# 5081

He causes the night to enter the day and causes the day to enter the night, and he is Knowing of that within the breasts.

# 5082

Believe in Allah and His Messenger and spend out of that in which He has made you successors. For those who have believed among you and spent, there will be a great reward.

# 5083

And why do you not believe in Allah while the Messenger invites you to believe in your Lord and He has taken your covenant, if you should [truly] be believers?

# 5084

It is He who sends down upon His Servant [Muhammad] verses of clear evidence that He may bring you out from darknesses into the light. And indeed, Allah is to you Kind and Merciful.

# 5085

And why do you not spend in the cause of Allah while to Allah belongs the heritage of the heavens and the earth? Not equal among you are those who spent before the conquest [of Makkah] and fought [and those who did so after it]. Those are greater in degree than they who spent afterwards and fought. But to all Allah has promised the best [reward]. And Allah, with what you do, is Acquainted.

# 5086

Who is it that would loan Allah a goodly loan so He will multiply it for him and he will have a noble reward?

# 5087

On the Day you see the believing men and believing women, their light proceeding before them and on their right, [it will be said], "Your good tidings today are [of] gardens beneath which rivers flow, wherein you will abide eternally." That is what is the great attainment.

# 5088

On the [same] Day the hypocrite men and hypocrite women will say to those who believed, "Wait for us that we may acquire some of your light." It will be said, "Go back behind you and seek light." And a wall will be placed between them with a door, its interior containing mercy, but on the outside of it is torment.

# 5089

The hypocrites will call to the believers, "Were we not with you?" They will say, "Yes, but you afflicted yourselves and awaited [misfortune for us] and doubted, and wishful thinking deluded you until there came the command of Allah. And the Deceiver deceived you concerning Allah.

# 5090

So today no ransom will be taken from you or from those who disbelieved. Your refuge is the Fire. It is most worthy of you, and wretched is the destination.

# 5091

Has the time not come for those who have believed that their hearts should become humbly submissive at the remembrance of Allah and what has come down of the truth? And let them not be like those who were given the Scripture before, and a long period passed over them, so their hearts hardened; and many of them are defiantly disobedient.

# 5092

Know that Allah gives life to the earth after its lifelessness. We have made clear to you the signs; perhaps you will understand.

# 5093

Indeed, the men who practice charity and the women who practice charity and [they who] have loaned Allah a goodly loan - it will be multiplied for them, and they will have a noble reward.

# 5094

And those who have believed in Allah and His messengers - those are [in the ranks of] the supporters of truth and the martyrs, with their Lord. For them is their reward and their light. But those who have disbelieved and denied Our verses - those are the companions of Hellfire.

# 5095

Know that the life of this world is but amusement and diversion and adornment and boasting to one another and competition in increase of wealth and children - like the example of a rain whose [resulting] plant growth pleases the tillers; then it dries and you see it turned yellow; then it becomes [scattered] debris. And in the Hereafter is severe punishment and forgiveness from Allah and approval. And what is the worldly life except the enjoyment of delusion.

# 5096

Race toward forgiveness from your Lord and a Garden whose width is like the width of the heavens and earth, prepared for those who believed in Allah and His messengers. That is the bounty of Allah which He gives to whom He wills, and Allah is the possessor of great bounty.

# 5097

No disaster strikes upon the earth or among yourselves except that it is in a register before We bring it into being - indeed that, for Allah, is easy -

# 5098

In order that you not despair over what has eluded you and not exult [in pride] over what He has given you. And Allah does not like everyone self-deluded and boastful -

# 5099

[Those] who are stingy and enjoin upon people stinginess. And whoever turns away - then indeed, Allah is the Free of need, the Praiseworthy.

# 5100

We have already sent Our messengers with clear evidences and sent down with them the Scripture and the balance that the people may maintain [their affairs] in justice.
