And We sent down iron, wherein is great military might and benefits for the people, and so that Allah may make evident those who support Him and His messengers unseen. Indeed, Allah is Powerful and Exalted in Might.

# 5101

And We have already sent Noah and Abraham and placed in their descendants prophethood and scripture; and among them is he who is guided, but many of them are defiantly disobedient.

# 5102

Then We sent following their footsteps Our messengers and followed [them] with Jesus, the son of Mary, and gave him the Gospel. And We placed in the hearts of those who followed him compassion and mercy and monasticism, which they innovated; We did not prescribe it for them except [that they did so] seeking the approval of Allah. But they did not observe it with due observance. So We gave the ones who believed among them their reward, but many of them are defiantly disobedient.

# 5103

O you who have believed, fear Allah and believe in His Messenger; He will [then] give you a double portion of His mercy and make for you a light by which you will walk and forgive you; and Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5104

[This is] so that the People of the Scripture may know that they are not able [to obtain] anything from the bounty of Allah and that [all] bounty is in the hand of Allah; He gives it to whom He wills. And Allah is the possessor of great bounty.

# 5105

Certainly has Allah heard the speech of the one who argues with you, [O Muhammad], concerning her husband and directs her complaint to Allah. And Allah hears your dialogue; indeed, Allah is Hearing and Seeing.

# 5106

Those who pronounce thihar among you [to separate] from their wives - they are not [consequently] their mothers. Their mothers are none but those who gave birth to them. And indeed, they are saying an objectionable statement and a falsehood. But indeed, Allah is Pardoning and Forgiving.

# 5107

And those who pronounce thihar from their wives and then [wish to] go back on what they said - then [there must be] the freeing of a slave before they touch one another. That is what you are admonished thereby; and Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5108

And he who does not find [a slave] - then a fast for two months consecutively before they touch one another; and he who is unable - then the feeding of sixty poor persons. That is for you to believe [completely] in Allah and His Messenger; and those are the limits [set by] Allah. And for the disbelievers is a painful punishment.

# 5109

Indeed, those who oppose Allah and His Messenger are abased as those before them were abased. And We have certainly sent down verses of clear evidence. And for the disbelievers is a humiliating punishment.

# 5110

On the Day when Allah will resurrect them all and inform them of what they did. Allah had enumerated it, while they forgot it; and Allah is, over all things, Witness.

# 5111

Have you not considered that Allah knows what is in the heavens and what is on the earth? There is in no private conversation three but that He is the fourth of them, nor are there five but that He is the sixth of them - and no less than that and no more except that He is with them [in knowledge] wherever they are. Then He will inform them of what they did, on the Day of Resurrection. Indeed Allah is, of all things, Knowing.

# 5112

Have you not considered those who were forbidden from private conversation, then they return to that which they were forbidden and converse among themselves about sin and aggression and disobedience to the Messenger? And when they come to you, they greet you with that [word] by which Allah does not greet you and say among themselves, "Why does Allah not punish us for what we say?" Sufficient for them is Hell, which they will [enter to] burn, and wretched is the destination.

# 5113

O you who have believed, when you converse privately, do not converse about sin and aggression and disobedience to the Messenger but converse about righteousness and piety. And fear Allah, to whom you will be gathered.

# 5114

Private conversation is only from Satan that he may grieve those who have believed, but he will not harm them at all except by permission of Allah. And upon Allah let the believers rely.

# 5115

O you who have believed, when you are told, "Space yourselves" in assemblies, then make space; Allah will make space for you. And when you are told, "Arise," then arise; Allah will raise those who have believed among you and those who were given knowledge, by degrees. And Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5116

O you who have believed, when you [wish to] privately consult the Messenger, present before your consultation a charity. That is better for you and purer. But if you find not [the means] - then indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5117

Have you feared to present before your consultation charities? Then when you do not and Allah has forgiven you, then [at least] establish prayer and give zakah and obey Allah and His Messenger. And Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5118

Have you not considered those who make allies of a people with whom Allah has become angry? They are neither of you nor of them, and they swear to untruth while they know [they are lying].

# 5119

Allah has prepared for them a severe punishment. Indeed, it was evil that they were doing.

# 5120

They took their [false] oaths as a cover, so they averted [people] from the way of Allah, and for them is a humiliating punishment.

# 5121

Never will their wealth or their children avail them against Allah at all. Those are the companions of the Fire; they will abide therein eternally

# 5122

On the Day Allah will resurrect them all, and they will swear to Him as they swear to you and think that they are [standing] on something. Unquestionably, it is they who are the liars.

# 5123

Satan has overcome them and made them forget the remembrance of Allah. Those are the party of Satan. Unquestionably, the party of Satan - they will be the losers.

# 5124

Indeed, the ones who oppose Allah and His Messenger - those will be among the most humbled.

# 5125

Allah has written, "I will surely overcome, I and My messengers." Indeed, Allah is Powerful and Exalted in Might.

# 5126

You will not find a people who believe in Allah and the Last Day having affection for those who oppose Allah and His Messenger, even if they were their fathers or their sons or their brothers or their kindred. Those - He has decreed within their hearts faith and supported them with spirit from Him. And We will admit them to gardens beneath which rivers flow, wherein they abide eternally. Allah is pleased with them, and they are pleased with Him - those are the party of Allah. Unquestionably, the party of Allah - they are the successful.

# 5127

Whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth exalts Allah, and He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5128

It is He who expelled the ones who disbelieved among the People of the Scripture from their homes at the first gathering. You did not think they would leave, and they thought that their fortresses would protect them from Allah; but [the decree of] Allah came upon them from where they had not expected, and He cast terror into their hearts [so] they destroyed their houses by their [own] hands and the hands of the believers. So take warning, O people of vision.

# 5129

And if not that Allah had decreed for them evacuation, He would have punished them in [this] world, and for them in the Hereafter is the punishment of the Fire.

# 5130

That is because they opposed Allah and His Messenger. And whoever opposes Allah - then indeed, Allah is severe in penalty.

# 5131

Whatever you have cut down of [their] palm trees or left standing on their trunks - it was by permission of Allah and so He would disgrace the defiantly disobedient.

# 5132

And what Allah restored [of property] to His Messenger from them - you did not spur for it [in an expedition] any horses or camels, but Allah gives His messengers power over whom He wills, and Allah is over all things competent.

# 5133

And what Allah restored to His Messenger from the people of the towns - it is for Allah and for the Messenger and for [his] near relatives and orphans and the [stranded] traveler - so that it will not be a perpetual distribution among the rich from among you. And whatever the Messenger has given you - take; and what he has forbidden you - refrain from. And fear Allah; indeed, Allah is severe in penalty.

# 5134

For the poor emigrants who were expelled from their homes and their properties, seeking bounty from Allah and [His] approval and supporting Allah and His Messenger, [there is also a share]. Those are the truthful.

# 5135

And [also for] those who were settled in al-Madinah and [adopted] the faith before them. They love those who emigrated to them and find not any want in their breasts of what the emigrants were given but give [them] preference over themselves, even though they are in privation. And whoever is protected from the stinginess of his soul - it is those who will be the successful.

# 5136

And [there is a share for] those who came after them, saying, "Our Lord, forgive us and our brothers who preceded us in faith and put not in our hearts [any] resentment toward those who have believed. Our Lord, indeed You are Kind and Merciful."

# 5137

Have you not considered those who practice hypocrisy, saying to their brothers who have disbelieved among the People of the Scripture, "If you are expelled, we will surely leave with you, and we will not obey, in regard to you, anyone - ever; and if you are fought, we will surely aid you." But Allah testifies that they are liars.

# 5138

If they are expelled, they will not leave with them, and if they are fought, they will not aid them. And [even] if they should aid them, they will surely turn their backs; then [thereafter] they will not be aided.

# 5139

You [believers] are more fearful within their breasts than Allah. That is because they are a people who do not understand.

# 5140

They will not fight you all except within fortified cities or from behind walls. Their violence among themselves is severe. You think they are together, but their hearts are diverse. That is because they are a people who do not reason.

# 5141

[Theirs is] like the example of those shortly before them: they tasted the bad consequence of their affair, and they will have a painful punishment.

# 5142

[The hypocrites are] like the example of Satan when he says to man, "Disbelieve." But when he disbelieves, he says, "Indeed, I am disassociated from you. Indeed, I fear Allah, Lord of the worlds."

# 5143

So the outcome for both of them is that they will be in the Fire, abiding eternally therein. And that is the recompense of the wrong-doers.

# 5144

O you who have believed, fear Allah. And let every soul look to what it has put forth for tomorrow - and fear Allah. Indeed, Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5145

And be not like those who forgot Allah, so He made them forget themselves. Those are the defiantly disobedient.

# 5146

Not equal are the companions of the Fire and the companions of Paradise. The companions of Paradise - they are the attainers [of success].

# 5147

If We had sent down this Qur'an upon a mountain, you would have seen it humbled and coming apart from fear of Allah. And these examples We present to the people that perhaps they will give thought.

# 5148

He is Allah, other than whom there is no deity, Knower of the unseen and the witnessed. He is the Entirely Merciful, the Especially Merciful.

# 5149

He is Allah, other than whom there is no deity, the Sovereign, the Pure, the Perfection, the Bestower of Faith, the Overseer, the Exalted in Might, the Compeller, the Superior. Exalted is Allah above whatever they associate with Him.

# 5150

He is Allah, the Creator, the Inventor, the Fashioner; to Him belong the best names. Whatever is in the heavens and earth is exalting Him. And He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5151

O you who have believed, do not take My enemies and your enemies as allies, extending to them affection while they have disbelieved in what came to you of the truth, having driven out the Prophet and yourselves [only] because you believe in Allah, your Lord. If you have come out for jihad in My cause and seeking means to My approval, [take them not as friends]. You confide to them affection, but I am most knowing of what you have concealed and what you have declared. And whoever does it among you has certainly strayed from the soundness of the way.

# 5152

If they gain dominance over you, they would be to you as enemies and extend against you their hands and their tongues with evil, and they wish you would disbelieve.

# 5153

Never will your relatives or your children benefit you; the Day of Resurrection He will judge between you. And Allah, of what you do, is Seeing.

# 5154

There has already been for you an excellent pattern in Abraham and those with him, when they said to their people, "Indeed, we are disassociated from you and from whatever you worship other than Allah. We have denied you, and there has appeared between us and you animosity and hatred forever until you believe in Allah alone" except for the saying of Abraham to his father, "I will surely ask forgiveness for you, but I have not [power to do] for you anything against Allah. Our Lord, upon You we have relied, and to You we have returned, and to You is the destination.

# 5155

Our Lord, make us not [objects of] torment for the disbelievers and forgive us, our Lord. Indeed, it is You who is the Exalted in Might, the Wise."

# 5156

There has certainly been for you in them an excellent pattern for anyone whose hope is in Allah and the Last Day. And whoever turns away - then indeed, Allah is the Free of need, the Praiseworthy.

# 5157

Perhaps Allah will put, between you and those to whom you have been enemies among them, affection. And Allah is competent, and Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5158

Allah does not forbid you from those who do not fight you because of religion and do not expel you from your homes - from being righteous toward them and acting justly toward them. Indeed, Allah loves those who act justly.

# 5159

Allah only forbids you from those who fight you because of religion and expel you from your homes and aid in your expulsion - [forbids] that you make allies of them. And whoever makes allies of them, then it is those who are the wrongdoers.

# 5160

O you who have believed, when the believing women come to you as emigrants, examine them. Allah is most knowing as to their faith. And if you know them to be believers, then do not return them to the disbelievers; they are not lawful [wives] for them, nor are they lawful [husbands] for them. But give the disbelievers what they have spent. And there is no blame upon you if you marry them when you have given them their due compensation. And hold not to marriage bonds with disbelieving women, but ask for what you have spent and let them ask for what they have spent. That is the judgement of Allah; He judges between you. And Allah is Knowing and Wise.

# 5161

And if you have lost any of your wives to the disbelievers and you subsequently obtain [something], then give those whose wives have gone the equivalent of what they had spent. And fear Allah, in whom you are believers.

# 5162

O Prophet, when the believing women come to you pledging to you that they will not associate anything with Allah, nor will they steal, nor will they commit unlawful sexual intercourse, nor will they kill their children, nor will they bring forth a slander they have invented between their arms and legs, nor will they disobey you in what is right - then accept their pledge and ask forgiveness for them of Allah. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5163

O you who have believed, do not make allies of a people with whom Allah has become angry. They have despaired of [reward in] the Hereafter just as the disbelievers have despaired of [meeting] the inhabitants of the graves.

# 5164

Whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth exalts Allah, and He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5165

O you who have believed, why do you say what you do not do?

# 5166

Great is hatred in the sight of Allah that you say what you do not do.

# 5167

Indeed, Allah loves those who fight in His cause in a row as though they are a [single] structure joined firmly.

# 5168

And [mention, O Muhammad], when Moses said to his people, "O my people, why do you harm me while you certainly know that I am the messenger of Allah to you?" And when they deviated, Allah caused their hearts to deviate. And Allah does not guide the defiantly disobedient people.

# 5169

And [mention] when Jesus, the son of Mary, said, "O children of Israel, indeed I am the messenger of Allah to you confirming what came before me of the Torah and bringing good tidings of a messenger to come after me, whose name is Ahmad." But when he came to them with clear evidences, they said, "This is obvious magic."

# 5170

And who is more unjust than one who invents about Allah untruth while he is being invited to Islam. And Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.

# 5171

They want to extinguish the light of Allah with their mouths, but Allah will perfect His light, although the disbelievers dislike it.

# 5172

It is He who sent His Messenger with guidance and the religion of truth to manifest it over all religion, although those who associate others with Allah dislike it.

# 5173

O you who have believed, shall I guide you to a transaction that will save you from a painful punishment?

# 5174

[It is that] you believe in Allah and His Messenger and strive in the cause of Allah with your wealth and your lives. That is best for you, if you should know.

# 5175

He will forgive for you your sins and admit you to gardens beneath which rivers flow and pleasant dwellings in gardens of perpetual residence. That is the great attainment.

# 5176

And [you will obtain] another [favor] that you love - victory from Allah and an imminent conquest; and give good tidings to the believers.

# 5177

O you who have believed, be supporters of Allah, as when Jesus, the son of Mary, said to the disciples, "Who are my supporters for Allah?" The disciples said, "We are supporters of Allah." And a faction of the Children of Israel believed and a faction disbelieved. So We supported those who believed against their enemy, and they became dominant.

# 5178

Whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth is exalting Allah, the Sovereign, the Pure, the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5179

It is He who has sent among the unlettered a Messenger from themselves reciting to them His verses and purifying them and teaching them the Book and wisdom - although they were before in clear error -

# 5180

And [to] others of them who have not yet joined them. And He is the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5181

That is the bounty of Allah, which He gives to whom He wills, and Allah is the possessor of great bounty.

# 5182

The example of those who were entrusted with the Torah and then did not take it on is like that of a donkey who carries volumes [of books]. Wretched is the example of the people who deny the signs of Allah. And Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.

# 5183

Say, "O you who are Jews, if you claim that you are allies of Allah, excluding the [other] people, then wish for death, if you should be truthful."

# 5184

But they will not wish for it, ever, because of what their hands have put forth. And Allah is Knowing of the wrongdoers.

# 5185

Say, "Indeed, the death from which you flee - indeed, it will meet you. Then you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, and He will inform you about what you used to do."

# 5186

O you who have believed, when [the adhan] is called for the prayer on the day of Jumu'ah [Friday], then proceed to the remembrance of Allah and leave trade. That is better for you, if you only knew.

# 5187

And when the prayer has been concluded, disperse within the land and seek from the bounty of Allah, and remember Allah often that you may succeed.

# 5188

But when they saw a transaction or a diversion, [O Muhammad], they rushed to it and left you standing. Say, "What is with Allah is better than diversion and than a transaction, and Allah is the best of providers."

# 5189

When the hypocrites come to you, [O Muhammad], they say, "We testify that you are the Messenger of Allah." And Allah knows that you are His Messenger, and Allah testifies that the hypocrites are liars.

# 5190

They have taken their oaths as a cover, so they averted [people] from the way of Allah. Indeed, it was evil that they were doing.

# 5191

That is because they believed, and then they disbelieved; so their hearts were sealed over, and they do not understand.

# 5192

And when you see them, their forms please you, and if they speak, you listen to their speech. [They are] as if they were pieces of wood propped up - they think that every shout is against them. They are the enemy, so beware of them. May Allah destroy them; how are they deluded?

# 5193

And when it is said to them, "Come, the Messenger of Allah will ask forgiveness for you," they turn their heads aside and you see them evading while they are arrogant.

# 5194

It is all the same for them whether you ask forgiveness for them or do not ask forgiveness for them; never will Allah forgive them. Indeed, Allah does not guide the defiantly disobedient people.

# 5195

They are the ones who say, "Do not spend on those who are with the Messenger of Allah until they disband." And to Allah belongs the depositories of the heavens and the earth, but the hypocrites do not understand.

# 5196

They say, "If we return to al-Madinah, the more honored [for power] will surely expel therefrom the more humble." And to Allah belongs [all] honor, and to His Messenger, and to the believers, but the hypocrites do not know.

# 5197

O you who have believed, let not your wealth and your children divert you from remembrance of Allah. And whoever does that - then those are the losers.

# 5198

And spend [in the way of Allah] from what We have provided you before death approaches one of you and he says, "My Lord, if only You would delay me for a brief term so I would give charity and be among the righteous."

# 5199

But never will Allah delay a soul when its time has come. And Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5200

Whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth is exalting Allah. To Him belongs dominion, and to Him belongs [all] praise, and He is over all things competent.

# 5201

It is He who created you, and among you is the disbeliever, and among you is the believer. And Allah, of what you do, is Seeing.

# 5202

He created the heavens and earth in truth and formed you and perfected your forms; and to Him is the [final] destination.

# 5203

He knows what is within the heavens and earth and knows what you conceal and what you declare. And Allah is Knowing of that within the breasts.

# 5204

Has there not come to you the news of those who disbelieved before? So they tasted the bad consequence of their affair, and they will have a painful punishment.

# 5205

That is because their messengers used to come to them with clear evidences, but they said, "Shall human beings guide us?" and disbelieved and turned away. And Allah dispensed [with them]; and Allah is Free of need and Praiseworthy.

# 5206

Those who disbelieve have claimed that they will never be resurrected. Say, "Yes, by my Lord, you will surely be resurrected; then you will surely be informed of what you did. And that, for Allah, is easy."

# 5207

So believe in Allah and His Messenger and the Qur'an which We have sent down. And Allah is Acquainted with what you do.

# 5208

The Day He will assemble you for the Day of Assembly - that is the Day of Deprivation. And whoever believes in Allah and does righteousness - He will remove from him his misdeeds and admit him to gardens beneath which rivers flow, wherein they will abide forever. That is the great attainment.

# 5209

But the ones who disbelieved and denied Our verses - those are the companions of the Fire, abiding eternally therein; and wretched is the destination.

# 5210

No disaster strikes except by permission of Allah. And whoever believes in Allah - He will guide his heart. And Allah is Knowing of all things.

# 5211

And obey Allah and obey the Messenger; but if you turn away - then upon Our Messenger is only [the duty of] clear notification.

# 5212

Allah - there is no deity except Him. And upon Allah let the believers rely.

# 5213

O you who have believed, indeed, among your wives and your children are enemies to you, so beware of them. But if you pardon and overlook and forgive - then indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5214

Your wealth and your children are but a trial, and Allah has with Him a great reward.

# 5215

So fear Allah as much as you are able and listen and obey and spend [in the way of Allah]; it is better for your selves. And whoever is protected from the stinginess of his soul - it is those who will be the successful.

# 5216

If you loan Allah a goodly loan, He will multiply it for you and forgive you. And Allah is Most Appreciative and Forbearing.

# 5217

Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, the Exalted in Might, the Wise.

# 5218

O Prophet, when you [Muslims] divorce women, divorce them for [the commencement of] their waiting period and keep count of the waiting period, and fear Allah, your Lord. Do not turn them out of their [husbands'] houses, nor should they [themselves] leave [during that period] unless they are committing a clear immorality. And those are the limits [set by] Allah. And whoever transgresses the limits of Allah has certainly wronged himself. You know not; perhaps Allah will bring about after that a [different] matter.

# 5219

And when they have [nearly] fulfilled their term, either retain them according to acceptable terms or part with them according to acceptable terms. And bring to witness two just men from among you and establish the testimony for [the acceptance of] Allah. That is instructed to whoever should believe in Allah and the Last day. And whoever fears Allah - He will make for him a way out

# 5220

And will provide for him from where he does not expect. And whoever relies upon Allah - then He is sufficient for him. Indeed, Allah will accomplish His purpose. Allah has already set for everything a [decreed] extent.

# 5221

And those who no longer expect menstruation among your women - if you doubt, then their period is three months, and [also for] those who have not menstruated. And for those who are pregnant, their term is until they give birth. And whoever fears Allah - He will make for him of his matter ease.

# 5222

That is the command of Allah, which He has sent down to you; and whoever fears Allah - He will remove for him his misdeeds and make great for him his reward.

# 5223

Lodge them [in a section] of where you dwell out of your means and do not harm them in order to oppress them. And if they should be pregnant, then spend on them until they give birth. And if they breastfeed for you, then give them their payment and confer among yourselves in the acceptable way; but if you are in discord, then there may breastfeed for the father another woman.

# 5224

Let a man of wealth spend from his wealth, and he whose provision is restricted - let him spend from what Allah has given him. Allah does not charge a soul except [according to] what He has given it. Allah will bring about, after hardship, ease.

# 5225

And how many a city was insolent toward the command of its Lord and His messengers, so We took it to severe account and punished it with a terrible punishment.

# 5226

And it tasted the bad consequence of its affair, and the outcome of its affair was loss.

# 5227

Allah has prepared for them a severe punishment; so fear Allah, O you of understanding who have believed. Allah has sent down to you the Qur'an.

# 5228

[He sent] a Messenger [Muhammad] reciting to you the distinct verses of Allah that He may bring out those who believe and do righteous deeds from darknesses into the light. And whoever believes in Allah and does righteousness - He will admit him into gardens beneath which rivers flow to abide therein forever. Allah will have perfected for him a provision.

# 5229

It is Allah who has created seven heavens and of the earth, the like of them. [His] command descends among them so you may know that Allah is over all things competent and that Allah has encompassed all things in knowledge.

# 5230

O Prophet, why do you prohibit [yourself from] what Allah has made lawful for you, seeking the approval of your wives? And Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5231

Allah has already ordained for you [Muslims] the dissolution of your oaths. And Allah is your protector, and He is the Knowing, the Wise.

# 5232

And [remember] when the Prophet confided to one of his wives a statement; and when she informed [another] of it and Allah showed it to him, he made known part of it and ignored a part. And when he informed her about it, she said, "Who told you this?" He said, "I was informed by the Knowing, the Acquainted."

# 5233

If you two [wives] repent to Allah, [it is best], for your hearts have deviated. But if you cooperate against him - then indeed Allah is his protector, and Gabriel and the righteous of the believers and the angels, moreover, are [his] assistants.

# 5234

Perhaps his Lord, if he divorced you [all], would substitute for him wives better than you - submitting [to Allah], believing, devoutly obedient, repentant, worshipping, and traveling - [ones] previously married and virgins.

# 5235

O you who have believed, protect yourselves and your families from a Fire whose fuel is people and stones, over which are [appointed] angels, harsh and severe; they do not disobey Allah in what He commands them but do what they are commanded.

# 5236

O you who have disbelieved, make no excuses that Day. You will only be recompensed for what you used to do.

# 5237

O you who have believed, repent to Allah with sincere repentance. Perhaps your Lord will remove from you your misdeeds and admit you into gardens beneath which rivers flow [on] the Day when Allah will not disgrace the Prophet and those who believed with him. Their light will proceed before them and on their right; they will say, "Our Lord, perfect for us our light and forgive us. Indeed, You are over all things competent."

# 5238

O Prophet, strive against the disbelievers and the hypocrites and be harsh upon them. And their refuge is Hell, and wretched is the destination.

# 5239

Allah presents an example of those who disbelieved: the wife of Noah and the wife of Lot. They were under two of Our righteous servants but betrayed them, so those prophets did not avail them from Allah at all, and it was said, "Enter the Fire with those who enter."

# 5240

And Allah presents an example of those who believed: the wife of Pharaoh, when she said, "My Lord, build for me near You a house in Paradise and save me from Pharaoh and his deeds and save me from the wrongdoing people."

# 5241

And [the example of] Mary, the daughter of 'Imran, who guarded her chastity, so We blew into [her garment] through Our angel, and she believed in the words of her Lord and His scriptures and was of the devoutly obedient.

# 5242

Blessed is He in whose hand is dominion, and He is over all things competent -

# 5243

[He] who created death and life to test you [as to] which of you is best in deed - and He is the Exalted in Might, the Forgiving -

# 5244

[And] who created seven heavens in layers. You do not see in the creation of the Most Merciful any inconsistency. So return [your] vision [to the sky]; do you see any breaks?

# 5245

Then return [your] vision twice again. [Your] vision will return to you humbled while it is fatigued.

# 5246

And We have certainly beautified the nearest heaven with stars and have made [from] them what is thrown at the devils and have prepared for them the punishment of the Blaze.

# 5247

And for those who disbelieved in their Lord is the punishment of Hell, and wretched is the destination.

# 5248

When they are thrown into it, they hear from it a [dreadful] inhaling while it boils up.

# 5249

It almost bursts with rage. Every time a company is thrown into it, its keepers ask them, "Did there not come to you a warner?"

# 5250

They will say," Yes, a warner had come to us, but we denied and said, 'Allah has not sent down anything. You are not but in great error.'"

# 5251

And they will say, "If only we had been listening or reasoning, we would not be among the companions of the Blaze."

# 5252

And they will admit their sin, so [it is] alienation for the companions of the Blaze.

# 5253

Indeed, those who fear their Lord unseen will have forgiveness and great reward.

# 5254

And conceal your speech or publicize it; indeed, He is Knowing of that within the breasts.

# 5255

Does He who created not know, while He is the Subtle, the Acquainted?

# 5256

It is He who made the earth tame for you - so walk among its slopes and eat of His provision - and to Him is the resurrection.

# 5257

Do you feel secure that He who [holds authority] in the heaven would not cause the earth to swallow you and suddenly it would sway?

# 5258

Or do you feel secure that He who [holds authority] in the heaven would not send against you a storm of stones? Then you would know how [severe] was My warning.

# 5259

And already had those before them denied, and how [terrible] was My reproach.

# 5260

Do they not see the birds above them with wings outspread and [sometimes] folded in? None holds them [aloft] except the Most Merciful. Indeed He is, of all things, Seeing.

# 5261

Or who is it that could be an army for you to aid you other than the Most Merciful? The disbelievers are not but in delusion.

# 5262

Or who is it that could provide for you if He withheld His provision? But they have persisted in insolence and aversion.

# 5263

Then is one who walks fallen on his face better guided or one who walks erect on a straight path?

# 5264

Say, "It is He who has produced you and made for you hearing and vision and hearts; little are you grateful."

# 5265

Say, "It is He who has multiplied you throughout the earth, and to Him you will be gathered."

# 5266

And they say, "When is this promise, if you should be truthful?"

# 5267

Say, "The knowledge is only with Allah, and I am only a clear warner."

# 5268

But when they see it approaching, the faces of those who disbelieve will be distressed, and it will be said, "This is that for which you used to call."

# 5269

Say, [O Muhammad], "Have you considered: whether Allah should cause my death and those with me or have mercy upon us, who can protect the disbelievers from a painful punishment?"

# 5270

Say, "He is the Most Merciful; we have believed in Him, and upon Him we have relied. And you will [come to] know who it is that is in clear error."

# 5271

Say, "Have you considered: if your water was to become sunken [into the earth], then who could bring you flowing water?"

# 5272

Nun. By the pen and what they inscribe,

# 5273

You are not, [O Muhammad], by the favor of your Lord, a madman.

# 5274

And indeed, for you is a reward uninterrupted.

# 5275

And indeed, you are of a great moral character.

# 5276

So you will see and they will see

# 5277

Which of you is the afflicted [by a devil].

# 5278

Indeed, your Lord is most knowing of who has gone astray from His way, and He is most knowing of the [rightly] guided.

# 5279

Then do not obey the deniers.

# 5280

They wish that you would soften [in your position], so they would soften [toward you].

# 5281

And do not obey every worthless habitual swearer

# 5282

[And] scorner, going about with malicious gossip -

# 5283

A preventer of good, transgressing and sinful,

# 5284

Cruel, moreover, and an illegitimate pretender.

# 5285

Because he is a possessor of wealth and children,

# 5286

When Our verses are recited to him, he says, "Legends of the former peoples."

# 5287

We will brand him upon the snout.

# 5288

Indeed, We have tried them as We tried the companions of the garden, when they swore to cut its fruit in the [early] morning

# 5289

Without making exception.

# 5290

So there came upon the garden an affliction from your Lord while they were asleep.

# 5291

And it became as though reaped.

# 5292

And they called one another at morning,

# 5293

[Saying], "Go early to your crop if you would cut the fruit."

# 5294

So they set out, while lowering their voices,

# 5295

[Saying], "There will surely not enter it today upon you [any] poor person."

# 5296

And they went early in determination, [assuming themselves] able.

# 5297

But when they saw it, they said, "Indeed, we are lost;

# 5298

Rather, we have been deprived."

# 5299

The most moderate of them said, "Did I not say to you, 'Why do you not exalt [Allah]?' "

# 5300

They said, "Exalted is our Lord! Indeed, we were wrongdoers."

# 5301

Then they approached one another, blaming each other.

# 5302

They said, "O woe to us; indeed we were transgressors.

# 5303

Perhaps our Lord will substitute for us [one] better than it. Indeed, we are toward our Lord desirous."

# 5304

Such is the punishment [of this world]. And the punishment of the Hereafter is greater, if they only knew.

# 5305

Indeed, for the righteous with their Lord are the Gardens of Pleasure.

# 5306

Then will We treat the Muslims like the criminals?

# 5307

What is [the matter] with you? How do you judge?

# 5308

Or do you have a scripture in which you learn

# 5309

That indeed for you is whatever you choose?

# 5310

Or do you have oaths [binding] upon Us, extending until the Day of Resurrection, that indeed for you is whatever you judge?

# 5311

Ask them which of them, for that [claim], is responsible.

# 5312

Or do they have partners? Then let them bring their partners, if they should be truthful.

# 5313

The Day the shin will be uncovered and they are invited to prostration but the disbelievers will not be able,

# 5314

Their eyes humbled, humiliation will cover them. And they used to be invited to prostration while they were sound.

# 5315

So leave Me, [O Muhammad], with [the matter of] whoever denies the Qur'an. We will progressively lead them [to punishment] from where they do not know.

# 5316

And I will give them time. Indeed, My plan is firm.

# 5317

Or do you ask of them a payment, so they are by debt burdened down?

# 5318

Or have they [knowledge of] the unseen, so they write [it] down?

# 5319

Then be patient for the decision of your Lord, [O Muhammad], and be not like the companion of the fish when he called out while he was distressed.

# 5320

If not that a favor from his Lord overtook him, he would have been thrown onto the naked shore while he was censured.

# 5321

And his Lord chose him and made him of the righteous.

# 5322

And indeed, those who disbelieve would almost make you slip with their eyes when they hear the message, and they say, "Indeed, he is mad."

# 5323

But it is not except a reminder to the worlds.

# 5324

The Inevitable Reality -

# 5325

What is the Inevitable Reality?

# 5326

And what can make you know what is the Inevitable Reality?

# 5327

Thamud and 'Aad denied the Striking Calamity.

# 5328

So as for Thamud, they were destroyed by the overpowering [blast].

# 5329

And as for 'Aad, they were destroyed by a screaming, violent wind

# 5330

Which Allah imposed upon them for seven nights and eight days in succession, so you would see the people therein fallen as if they were hollow trunks of palm trees.

# 5331

Then do you see of them any remains?

# 5332

And there came Pharaoh and those before him and the overturned cities with sin.

# 5333

And they disobeyed the messenger of their Lord, so He seized them with a seizure exceeding [in severity].

# 5334

Indeed, when the water overflowed, We carried your ancestors in the sailing ship

# 5335

That We might make it for you a reminder and [that] a conscious ear would be conscious of it.

# 5336

Then when the Horn is blown with one blast

# 5337

And the earth and the mountains are lifted and leveled with one blow -

# 5338

Then on that Day, the Resurrection will occur,

# 5339

And the heaven will split [open], for that Day it is infirm.

# 5340

And the angels are at its edges. And there will bear the Throne of your Lord above them, that Day, eight [of them].

# 5341

That Day, you will be exhibited [for judgement]; not hidden among you is anything concealed.

# 5342

So as for he who is given his record in his right hand, he will say, "Here, read my record!

# 5343

Indeed, I was certain that I would be meeting my account."

# 5344

So he will be in a pleasant life -

# 5345

In an elevated garden,

# 5346

Its [fruit] to be picked hanging near.

# 5347

[They will be told], "Eat and drink in satisfaction for what you put forth in the days past."

# 5348

But as for he who is given his record in his left hand, he will say, "Oh, I wish I had not been given my record

# 5349

And had not known what is my account.

# 5350

I wish my death had been the decisive one.

# 5351

My wealth has not availed me.

# 5352

Gone from me is my authority."

# 5353

[Allah will say], "Seize him and shackle him.

# 5354

Then into Hellfire drive him.

# 5355

Then into a chain whose length is seventy cubits insert him."

# 5356

Indeed, he did not used to believe in Allah, the Most Great,

# 5357

Nor did he encourage the feeding of the poor.

# 5358

So there is not for him here this Day any devoted friend

# 5359

Nor any food except from the discharge of wounds;

# 5360

None will eat it except the sinners.

# 5361

So I swear by what you see

# 5362

And what you do not see

# 5363

[That] indeed, the Qur'an is the word of a noble Messenger.

# 5364

And it is not the word of a poet; little do you believe.

# 5365

Nor the word of a soothsayer; little do you remember.

# 5366

[It is] a revelation from the Lord of the worlds.

# 5367

And if Muhammad had made up about Us some [false] sayings,

# 5368

We would have seized him by the right hand;

# 5369

Then We would have cut from him the aorta.

# 5370

And there is no one of you who could prevent [Us] from him.

# 5371

And indeed, the Qur'an is a reminder for the righteous.

# 5372

And indeed, We know that among you are deniers.

# 5373

And indeed, it will be [a cause of] regret upon the disbelievers.

# 5374

And indeed, it is the truth of certainty.

# 5375

So exalt the name of your Lord, the Most Great.

# 5376

A supplicant asked for a punishment bound to happen

# 5377

To the disbelievers; of it there is no preventer.

# 5378

[It is] from Allah, owner of the ways of ascent.

# 5379

The angels and the Spirit will ascend to Him during a Day the extent of which is fifty thousand years.

# 5380

So be patient with gracious patience.

# 5381

Indeed, they see it [as] distant,

# 5382

But We see it [as] near.

# 5383

On the Day the sky will be like murky oil,

# 5384

And the mountains will be like wool,

# 5385

And no friend will ask [anything of] a friend,

# 5386

They will be shown each other. The criminal will wish that he could be ransomed from the punishment of that Day by his children

# 5387

And his wife and his brother

# 5388

And his nearest kindred who shelter him

# 5389

And whoever is on earth entirely [so] then it could save him.

# 5390

No! Indeed, it is the Flame [of Hell],

# 5391

A remover of exteriors.

# 5392

It invites he who turned his back [on truth] and went away [from obedience]

# 5393

And collected [wealth] and hoarded.

# 5394

Indeed, mankind was created anxious:

# 5395

When evil touches him, impatient,

# 5396

And when good touches him, withholding [of it],

# 5397

Except the observers of prayer -

# 5398

Those who are constant in their prayer

# 5399

And those within whose wealth is a known right

# 5400

For the petitioner and the deprived -

# 5401

And those who believe in the Day of Recompense

# 5402

And those who are fearful of the punishment of their Lord -

# 5403

Indeed, the punishment of their Lord is not that from which one is safe -

# 5404

And those who guard their private parts

# 5405

Except from their wives or those their right hands possess, for indeed, they are not to be blamed -

# 5406

But whoever seeks beyond that, then they are the transgressors -

# 5407

And those who are to their trusts and promises attentive

# 5408

And those who are in their testimonies upright

# 5409

And those who [carefully] maintain their prayer:

# 5410

They will be in gardens, honored.

# 5411

So what is [the matter] with those who disbelieve, hastening [from] before you, [O Muhammad],

# 5412

[To sit] on [your] right and [your] left in separate groups?

# 5413

Does every person among them aspire to enter a garden of pleasure?

# 5414

No! Indeed, We have created them from that which they know.

# 5415

So I swear by the Lord of [all] risings and settings that indeed We are able

# 5416

To replace them with better than them; and We are not to be outdone.

# 5417

So leave them to converse vainly and amuse themselves until they meet their Day which they are promised -

# 5418

The Day they will emerge from the graves rapidly as if they were, toward an erected idol, hastening.

# 5419

Their eyes humbled, humiliation will cover them. That is the Day which they had been promised.

# 5420

Indeed, We sent Noah to his people, [saying], "Warn your people before there comes to them a painful punishment."

# 5421

He said, "O my people, indeed I am to you a clear warner,

# 5422

[Saying], 'Worship Allah, fear Him and obey me.

# 5423

Allah will forgive you of your sins and delay you for a specified term. Indeed, the time [set by] Allah, when it comes, will not be delayed, if you only knew.' "

# 5424

He said, "My Lord, indeed I invited my people [to truth] night and day.

# 5425

But my invitation increased them not except in flight.

# 5426

And indeed, every time I invited them that You may forgive them, they put their fingers in their ears, covered themselves with their garments, persisted, and were arrogant with [great] arrogance.

# 5427

Then I invited them publicly.

# 5428

Then I announced to them and [also] confided to them secretly

# 5429

And said, 'Ask forgiveness of your Lord. Indeed, He is ever a Perpetual Forgiver.

# 5430

He will send [rain from] the sky upon you in [continuing] showers

# 5431

And give you increase in wealth and children and provide for you gardens and provide for you rivers.

# 5432

What is [the matter] with you that you do not attribute to Allah [due] grandeur

# 5433

While He has created you in stages?

# 5434

Do you not consider how Allah has created seven heavens in layers

# 5435

And made the moon therein a [reflected] light and made the sun a burning lamp?

# 5436

And Allah has caused you to grow from the earth a [progressive] growth.

# 5437

Then He will return you into it and extract you [another] extraction.

# 5438

And Allah has made for you the earth an expanse

# 5439

That you may follow therein roads of passage.' "

# 5440

Noah said, "My Lord, indeed they have disobeyed me and followed him whose wealth and children will not increase him except in loss.

# 5441

And they conspired an immense conspiracy.

# 5442

And said, 'Never leave your gods and never leave Wadd or Suwa' or Yaghuth and Ya'uq and Nasr.

# 5443

And already they have misled many. And, [my Lord], do not increase the wrongdoers except in error."

# 5444

Because of their sins they were drowned and put into the Fire, and they found not for themselves besides Allah [any] helpers.

# 5445

And Noah said, "My Lord, do not leave upon the earth from among the disbelievers an inhabitant.

# 5446

Indeed, if You leave them, they will mislead Your servants and not beget except [every] wicked one and [confirmed] disbeliever.

# 5447

My Lord, forgive me and my parents and whoever enters my house a believer and the believing men and believing women. And do not increase the wrongdoers except in destruction."

# 5448

Say, [O Muhammad], "It has been revealed to me that a group of the jinn listened and said, 'Indeed, we have heard an amazing Qur'an.

# 5449

It guides to the right course, and we have believed in it. And we will never associate with our Lord anyone.

# 5450

And [it teaches] that exalted is the nobleness of our Lord; He has not taken a wife or a son

# 5451

And that our foolish one has been saying about Allah an excessive transgression.

# 5452

And we had thought that mankind and the jinn would never speak about Allah a lie.

# 5453

And there were men from mankind who sought refuge in men from the jinn, so they [only] increased them in burden.

# 5454

And they had thought, as you thought, that Allah would never send anyone [as a messenger].

# 5455

And we have sought [to reach] the heaven but found it filled with powerful guards and burning flames.

# 5456

And we used to sit therein in positions for hearing, but whoever listens now will find a burning flame lying in wait for him.

# 5457

And we do not know [therefore] whether evil is intended for those on earth or whether their Lord intends for them a right course.

# 5458

And among us are the righteous, and among us are [others] not so; we were [of] divided ways.

# 5459

And we have become certain that we will never cause failure to Allah upon earth, nor can we escape Him by flight.

# 5460

And when we heard the guidance, we believed in it. And whoever believes in his Lord will not fear deprivation or burden.

# 5461

And among us are Muslims [in submission to Allah], and among us are the unjust. And whoever has become Muslim - those have sought out the right course.

# 5462

But as for the unjust, they will be, for Hell, firewood.'

# 5463

And [Allah revealed] that if they had remained straight on the way, We would have given them abundant provision

# 5464

So We might test them therein. And whoever turns away from the remembrance of his Lord He will put into arduous punishment.

# 5465

And [He revealed] that the masjids are for Allah, so do not invoke with Allah anyone.

# 5466

And that when the Servant of Allah stood up supplicating Him, they almost became about him a compacted mass."

# 5467

Say, [O Muhammad], "I only invoke my Lord and do not associate with Him anyone."

# 5468

Say, "Indeed, I do not possess for you [the power of] harm or right direction."

# 5469

Say, "Indeed, there will never protect me from Allah anyone [if I should disobey], nor will I find in other than Him a refuge.

# 5470

But [I have for you] only notification from Allah, and His messages." And whoever disobeys Allah and His Messenger - then indeed, for him is the fire of Hell; they will abide therein forever.

# 5471

[The disbelievers continue] until, when they see that which they are promised, then they will know who is weaker in helpers and less in number.

# 5472

Say, "I do not know if what you are promised is near or if my Lord will grant for it a [long] period."

# 5473

[He is] Knower of the unseen, and He does not disclose His [knowledge of the] unseen to anyone

# 5474

Except whom He has approved of messengers, and indeed, He sends before each messenger and behind him observers

# 5475

That he may know that they have conveyed the messages of their Lord; and He has encompassed whatever is with them and has enumerated all things in number.

# 5476

O you who wraps himself [in clothing],

# 5477

Arise [to pray] the night, except for a little -

# 5478

Half of it - or subtract from it a little

# 5479

Or add to it, and recite the Qur'an with measured recitation.

# 5480

Indeed, We will cast upon you a heavy word.

# 5481

Indeed, the hours of the night are more effective for concurrence [of heart and tongue] and more suitable for words.

# 5482

Indeed, for you by day is prolonged occupation.

# 5483

And remember the name of your Lord and devote yourself to Him with [complete] devotion.

# 5484

[He is] the Lord of the East and the West; there is no deity except Him, so take Him as Disposer of [your] affairs.

# 5485

And be patient over what they say and avoid them with gracious avoidance.

# 5486

And leave Me with [the matter of] the deniers, those of ease [in life], and allow them respite a little.

# 5487

Indeed, with Us [for them] are shackles and burning fire

# 5488

And food that chokes and a painful punishment -

# 5489

On the Day the earth and the mountains will convulse and the mountains will become a heap of sand pouring down.

# 5490

Indeed, We have sent to you a Messenger as a witness upon you just as We sent to Pharaoh a messenger.

# 5491

But Pharaoh disobeyed the messenger, so We seized him with a ruinous seizure.

# 5492

Then how can you fear, if you disbelieve, a Day that will make the children white- haired?

# 5493

The heaven will break apart therefrom; ever is His promise fulfilled.

# 5494

Indeed, this is a reminder, so whoever wills may take to his Lord a way.

# 5495

Indeed, your Lord knows, [O Muhammad], that you stand [in prayer] almost two thirds of the night or half of it or a third of it, and [so do] a group of those with you. And Allah determines [the extent of] the night and the day. He has known that you [Muslims] will not be able to do it and has turned to you in forgiveness, so recite what is easy [for you] of the Qur'an. He has known that there will be among you those who are ill and others traveling throughout the land seeking [something] of the bounty of Allah and others fighting for the cause of Allah. So recite what is easy from it and establish prayer and give zakah and loan Allah a goodly loan. And whatever good you put forward for yourselves - you will find it with Allah. It is better and greater in reward. And seek forgiveness of Allah. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

# 5496

O you who covers himself [with a garment],

# 5497

Arise and warn

# 5498

And your Lord glorify

# 5499

And your clothing purify

# 5500

And uncleanliness avoid

# 5501

And do not confer favor to acquire more

# 5502

But for your Lord be patient.

# 5503

And when the trumpet is blown,

# 5504

That Day will be a difficult day

# 5505

For the disbelievers - not easy.

# 5506

Leave Me with the one I created alone

# 5507

And to whom I granted extensive wealth

# 5508

And children present [with him]

# 5509

And spread [everything] before him, easing [his life].

# 5510

Then he desires that I should add more.

# 5511

No! Indeed, he has been toward Our verses obstinate.

# 5512

I will cover him with arduous torment.

# 5513

Indeed, he thought and deliberated.

# 5514

So may he be destroyed [for] how he deliberated.

# 5515

Then may he be destroyed [for] how he deliberated.

# 5516

Then he considered [again];

# 5517

Then he frowned and scowled;

# 5518

Then he turned back and was arrogant

# 5519

And said, "This is not but magic imitated [from others].

# 5520

This is not but the word of a human being."

# 5521

I will drive him into Saqar.

# 5522

And what can make you know what is Saqar?

# 5523

It lets nothing remain and leaves nothing [unburned],

# 5524

Blackening the skins.

# 5525

Over it are nineteen [angels].

# 5526

And We have not made the keepers of the Fire except angels. And We have not made their number except as a trial for those who disbelieve - that those who were given the Scripture will be convinced and those who have believed will increase in faith and those who were given the Scripture and the believers will not doubt and that those in whose hearts is hypocrisy and the disbelievers will say, "What does Allah intend by this as an example?" Thus does Allah leave astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills. And none knows the soldiers of your Lord except Him. And mention of the Fire is not but a reminder to humanity.

# 5527

No! By the moon

# 5528

And [by] the night when it departs

# 5529

And [by] the morning when it brightens,

# 5530

Indeed, the Fire is of the greatest [afflictions]

# 5531

As a warning to humanity -

# 5532

To whoever wills among you to proceed or stay behind.

# 5533

Every soul, for what it has earned, will be retained

# 5534

Except the companions of the right,

# 5535

[Who will be] in gardens, questioning each other

# 5536

About the criminals,

# 5537

[And asking them], "What put you into Saqar?"

# 5538

They will say, "We were not of those who prayed,

# 5539

Nor did we used to feed the poor.

# 5540

And we used to enter into vain discourse with those who engaged [in it],

# 5541

And we used to deny the Day of Recompense

# 5542

Until there came to us the certainty."

# 5543

So there will not benefit them the intercession of [any] intercessors.

# 5544

Then what is [the matter] with them that they are, from the reminder, turning away

# 5545

As if they were alarmed donkeys

# 5546

Fleeing from a lion?

# 5547

Rather, every person among them desires that he would be given scriptures spread about.

# 5548

No! But they do not fear the Hereafter.

# 5549

No! Indeed, the Qur'an is a reminder

# 5550

Then whoever wills will remember it.

# 5551

And they will not remember except that Allah wills. He is worthy of fear and adequate for [granting] forgiveness.

# 5552

I swear by the Day of Resurrection

# 5553

And I swear by the reproaching soul [to the certainty of resurrection].

# 5554

Does man think that We will not assemble his bones?

# 5555

Yes. [We are] Able [even] to proportion his fingertips.

# 5556

But man desires to continue in sin.

# 5557

He asks, "When is the Day of Resurrection?"

# 5558

So when vision is dazzled

# 5559

And the moon darkens

# 5560

And the sun and the moon are joined,

# 5561

Man will say on that Day, "Where is the [place of] escape?"

# 5562

No! There is no refuge.

# 5563

To your Lord, that Day, is the [place of] permanence.

# 5564

Man will be informed that Day of what he sent ahead and kept back.

# 5565

Rather, man, against himself, will be a witness,

# 5566

Even if he presents his excuses.

# 5567

Move not your tongue with it, [O Muhammad], to hasten with recitation of the Qur'an.

# 5568

Indeed, upon Us is its collection [in your heart] and [to make possible] its recitation.

# 5569

So when We have recited it [through Gabriel], then follow its recitation.

# 5570

Then upon Us is its clarification [to you].

# 5571

No! But you love the immediate

# 5572

And leave the Hereafter.

# 5573

[Some] faces, that Day, will be radiant,

# 5574

Looking at their Lord.

# 5575

And [some] faces, that Day, will be contorted,

# 5576

Expecting that there will be done to them [something] backbreaking.

# 5577

No! When the soul has reached the collar bones

# 5578

And it is said, "Who will cure [him]?"

# 5579

And the dying one is certain that it is the [time of] separation

# 5580

And the leg is wound about the leg,

# 5581

To your Lord, that Day, will be the procession.

# 5582

And the disbeliever had not believed, nor had he prayed.

# 5583

But [instead], he denied and turned away.

# 5584

And then he went to his people, swaggering [in pride].

# 5585

Woe to you, and woe!

# 5586

Then woe to you, and woe!

# 5587

Does man think that he will be left neglected?

# 5588

Had he not been a sperm from semen emitted?

# 5589

Then he was a clinging clot, and [Allah] created [his form] and proportioned [him]

# 5590

And made of him two mates, the male and the female.

# 5591

Is not that [Creator] Able to give life to the dead?

# 5592

Has there [not] come upon man a period of time when he was not a thing [even] mentioned?

# 5593

Indeed, We created man from a sperm-drop mixture that We may try him; and We made him hearing and seeing.

# 5594

Indeed, We guided him to the way, be he grateful or be he ungrateful.

# 5595

Indeed, We have prepared for the disbelievers chains and shackles and a blaze.

# 5596

Indeed, the righteous will drink from a cup [of wine] whose mixture is of Kafur,

# 5597

A spring of which the [righteous] servants of Allah will drink; they will make it gush forth in force [and abundance].

# 5598

They [are those who] fulfill [their] vows and fear a Day whose evil will be widespread.

# 5599

And they give food in spite of love for it to the needy, the orphan, and the captive,

# 5600

[Saying], "We feed you only for the countenance of Allah. We wish not from you reward or gratitude.

# 5601

Indeed, We fear from our Lord a Day austere and distressful."

# 5602

So Allah will protect them from the evil of that Day and give them radiance and happiness

# 5603

And will reward them for what they patiently endured [with] a garden [in Paradise] and silk [garments].

# 5604

[They will be] reclining therein on adorned couches. They will not see therein any [burning] sun or [freezing] cold.

# 5605

And near above them are its shades, and its [fruit] to be picked will be lowered in compliance.

# 5606

And there will be circulated among them vessels of silver and cups having been [created] clear [as glass],

# 5607

Clear glasses [made] from silver of which they have determined the measure.

# 5608

And they will be given to drink a cup [of wine] whose mixture is of ginger

# 5609

[From] a fountain within Paradise named Salsabeel.

# 5610

There will circulate among them young boys made eternal. When you see them, you would think them [as beautiful as] scattered pearls.

# 5611

And when you look there [in Paradise], you will see pleasure and great dominion.

# 5612

Upon the inhabitants will be green garments of fine silk and brocade. And they will be adorned with bracelets of silver, and their Lord will give them a purifying drink.

# 5613

[And it will be said], "Indeed, this is for you a reward, and your effort has been appreciated."

# 5614

Indeed, it is We who have sent down to you, [O Muhammad], the Qur'an progressively.

# 5615

So be patient for the decision of your Lord and do not obey from among them a sinner or ungrateful [disbeliever].

# 5616

And mention the name of your Lord [in prayer] morning and evening

# 5617

And during the night prostrate to Him and exalt Him a long [part of the] night.

# 5618

Indeed, these [disbelievers] love the immediate and leave behind them a grave Day.

# 5619

We have created them and strengthened their forms, and when We will, We can change their likenesses with [complete] alteration.

# 5620

Indeed, this is a reminder, so he who wills may take to his Lord a way.

# 5621

And you do not will except that Allah wills. Indeed, Allah is ever Knowing and Wise.

# 5622

He admits whom He wills into His mercy; but the wrongdoers - He has prepared for them a painful punishment.

# 5623

By those [winds] sent forth in gusts

# 5624

And the winds that blow violently

# 5625

And [by] the winds that spread [clouds]

# 5626

And those [angels] who bring criterion

# 5627

And those [angels] who deliver a message

# 5628

As justification or warning,

# 5629

Indeed, what you are promised is to occur.

# 5630

So when the stars are obliterated

# 5631

And when the heaven is opened

# 5632

And when the mountains are blown away

# 5633

And when the messengers' time has come...

# 5634

For what Day was it postponed?

# 5635

For the Day of Judgement.

# 5636

And what can make you know what is the Day of Judgement?

# 5637

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5638

Did We not destroy the former peoples?

# 5639

Then We will follow them with the later ones.

# 5640

Thus do We deal with the criminals.

# 5641

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5642

Did We not create you from a liquid disdained?

# 5643

And We placed it in a firm lodging

# 5644

For a known extent.

# 5645

And We determined [it], and excellent [are We] to determine.

# 5646

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5647

Have We not made the earth a container

# 5648

Of the living and the dead?

# 5649

And We placed therein lofty, firmly set mountains and have given you to drink sweet water.

# 5650

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5651

[They will be told], "Proceed to that which you used to deny.

# 5652

Proceed to a shadow [of smoke] having three columns

# 5653

[But having] no cool shade and availing not against the flame."

# 5654

Indeed, it throws sparks [as huge] as a fortress,

# 5655

As if they were yellowish [black] camels.

# 5656

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5657

This is a Day they will not speak,

# 5658

Nor will it be permitted for them to make an excuse.

# 5659

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5660

This is the Day of Judgement; We will have assembled you and the former peoples.

# 5661

So if you have a plan, then plan against Me.

# 5662

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5663

Indeed, the righteous will be among shades and springs

# 5664

And fruits from whatever they desire,

# 5665

[Being told], "Eat and drink in satisfaction for what you used to do."

# 5666

Indeed, We thus reward the doers of good.

# 5667

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5668

[O disbelievers], eat and enjoy yourselves a little; indeed, you are criminals.

# 5669

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5670

And when it is said to them, "Bow [in prayer]," they do not bow.

# 5671

Woe, that Day, to the deniers.

# 5672

Then in what statement after the Qur'an will they believe?

# 5673

About what are they asking one another?

# 5674

About the great news -

# 5675

That over which they are in disagreement.

# 5676

No! They are going to know.

# 5677

Then, no! They are going to know.

# 5678

Have We not made the earth a resting place?

# 5679

And the mountains as stakes?

# 5680

And We created you in pairs

# 5681

And made your sleep [a means for] rest

# 5682

And made the night as clothing

# 5683

And made the day for livelihood

# 5684

And constructed above you seven strong [heavens]

# 5685

And made [therein] a burning lamp

# 5686

And sent down, from the rain clouds, pouring water

# 5687

That We may bring forth thereby grain and vegetation

# 5688

And gardens of entwined growth.

# 5689

Indeed, the Day of Judgement is an appointed time -

# 5690

The Day the Horn is blown and you will come forth in multitudes

# 5691

And the heaven is opened and will become gateways

# 5692

And the mountains are removed and will be [but] a mirage.

# 5693

Indeed, Hell has been lying in wait

# 5694

For the transgressors, a place of return,

# 5695

In which they will remain for ages [unending].

# 5696

They will not taste therein [any] coolness or drink

# 5697

Except scalding water and [foul] purulence -

# 5698

An appropriate recompense.

# 5699

Indeed, they were not expecting an account

# 5700

And denied Our verses with [emphatic] denial.

# 5701

But all things We have enumerated in writing.

# 5702

"So taste [the penalty], and never will We increase you except in torment."

# 5703

Indeed, for the righteous is attainment -

# 5704

Gardens and grapevines

# 5705

And full-breasted [companions] of equal age

# 5706

And a full cup.

# 5707

No ill speech will they hear therein or any falsehood -

# 5708

[As] reward from your Lord, [a generous] gift [made due by] account,

# 5709

[From] the Lord of the heavens and the earth and whatever is between them, the Most Merciful. They possess not from Him [authority for] speech.

# 5710

The Day that the Spirit and the angels will stand in rows, they will not speak except for one whom the Most Merciful permits, and he will say what is correct.

# 5711

That is the True Day; so he who wills may take to his Lord a [way of] return.

# 5712

Indeed, We have warned you of a near punishment on the Day when a man will observe what his hands have put forth and the disbeliever will say, "Oh, I wish that I were dust!"

# 5713

By those [angels] who extract with violence

# 5714

And [by] those who remove with ease

# 5715

And [by] those who glide [as if] swimming

# 5716

And those who race each other in a race

# 5717

And those who arrange [each] matter,

# 5718

On the Day the blast [of the Horn] will convulse [creation],

# 5719

There will follow it the subsequent [one].

# 5720

Hearts, that Day, will tremble,

# 5721

Their eyes humbled.

# 5722

They are [presently] saying, "Will we indeed be returned to [our] former state [of life]?

# 5723

Even if we should be decayed bones?

# 5724

They say, "That, then, would be a losing return."

# 5725

Indeed, it will be but one shout,

# 5726

And suddenly they will be [alert] upon the earth's surface.

# 5727

Has there reached you the story of Moses? -

# 5728

When his Lord called to him in the sacred valley of Tuwa,

# 5729

"Go to Pharaoh. Indeed, he has transgressed.

# 5730

And say to him, 'Would you [be willing to] purify yourself

# 5731

And let me guide you to your Lord so you would fear [Him]?'"

# 5732

And he showed him the greatest sign,

# 5733

But Pharaoh denied and disobeyed.

# 5734

Then he turned his back, striving.

# 5735

And he gathered [his people] and called out

# 5736

And said, "I am your most exalted lord."

# 5737

So Allah seized him in exemplary punishment for the last and the first [transgression].

# 5738

Indeed in that is a warning for whoever would fear [Allah].

# 5739

Are you a more difficult creation or is the heaven? Allah constructed it.

# 5740

He raised its ceiling and proportioned it.

# 5741

And He darkened its night and extracted its brightness.

# 5742

And after that He spread the earth.

# 5743

He extracted from it its water and its pasture,

# 5744

And the mountains He set firmly

# 5745

As provision for you and your grazing livestock.

# 5746

But when there comes the greatest Overwhelming Calamity -

# 5747

The Day when man will remember that for which he strove,

# 5748

And Hellfire will be exposed for [all] those who see -

# 5749

So as for he who transgressed

# 5750

And preferred the life of the world,

# 5751

Then indeed, Hellfire will be [his] refuge.

# 5752

But as for he who feared the position of his Lord and prevented the soul from [unlawful] inclination,

# 5753

Then indeed, Paradise will be [his] refuge.

# 5754

They ask you, [O Muhammad], about the Hour: when is its arrival?

# 5755

In what [position] are you that you should mention it?

# 5756

To your Lord is its finality.

# 5757

You are only a warner for those who fear it.

# 5758

It will be, on the Day they see it, as though they had not remained [in the world] except for an afternoon or a morning thereof.

# 5759

The Prophet frowned and turned away

# 5760

Because there came to him the blind man, [interrupting].

# 5761

But what would make you perceive, [O Muhammad], that perhaps he might be purified

# 5762

Or be reminded and the remembrance would benefit him?

# 5763

As for he who thinks himself without need,

# 5764

To him you give attention.

# 5765

And not upon you [is any blame] if he will not be purified.

# 5766

But as for he who came to you striving [for knowledge]

# 5767

While he fears [Allah],

# 5768

From him you are distracted.

# 5769

No! Indeed, these verses are a reminder;

# 5770

So whoever wills may remember it.

# 5771

[It is recorded] in honored sheets,

# 5772

Exalted and purified,

# 5773

[Carried] by the hands of messenger-angels,

# 5774

Noble and dutiful.

# 5775

Cursed is man; how disbelieving is he.

# 5776

From what substance did He create him?

# 5777

From a sperm-drop He created him and destined for him;

# 5778

Then He eased the way for him;

# 5779

Then He causes his death and provides a grave for him.

# 5780

Then when He wills, He will resurrect him.

# 5781

No! Man has not yet accomplished what He commanded him.

# 5782

Then let mankind look at his food -

# 5783

How We poured down water in torrents,

# 5784

Then We broke open the earth, splitting [it with sprouts],

# 5785

And caused to grow within it grain

# 5786

And grapes and herbage

# 5787

And olive and palm trees

# 5788

And gardens of dense shrubbery

# 5789

And fruit and grass -

# 5790

[As] enjoyment for you and your grazing livestock.

# 5791

But when there comes the Deafening Blast

# 5792

On the Day a man will flee from his brother

# 5793

And his mother and his father

# 5794

And his wife and his children,

# 5795

For every man, that Day, will be a matter adequate for him.

# 5796

[Some] faces, that Day, will be bright -

# 5797

Laughing, rejoicing at good news.

# 5798

And [other] faces, that Day, will have upon them dust.

# 5799

Blackness will cover them.

# 5800

Those are the disbelievers, the wicked ones.

# 5801

When the sun is wrapped up [in darkness]

# 5802

And when the stars fall, dispersing,

# 5803

And when the mountains are removed

# 5804

And when full-term she-camels are neglected

# 5805

And when the wild beasts are gathered

# 5806

And when the seas are filled with flame

# 5807

And when the souls are paired

# 5808

And when the girl [who was] buried alive is asked

# 5809

For what sin she was killed

# 5810

And when the pages are made public

# 5811

And when the sky is stripped away

# 5812

And when Hellfire is set ablaze

# 5813

And when Paradise is brought near,

# 5814

A soul will [then] know what it has brought [with it].

# 5815

So I swear by the retreating stars -

# 5816

Those that run [their courses] and disappear -

# 5817

And by the night as it closes in

# 5818

And by the dawn when it breathes

# 5819

[That] indeed, the Qur'an is a word [conveyed by] a noble messenger

# 5820

[Who is] possessed of power and with the Owner of the Throne, secure [in position],

# 5821

Obeyed there [in the heavens] and trustworthy.

# 5822

And your companion is not [at all] mad.

# 5823

And he has already seen Gabriel in the clear horizon.

# 5824

And Muhammad is not a withholder of [knowledge of] the unseen.

# 5825

And the Qur'an is not the word of a devil, expelled [from the heavens].

# 5826

So where are you going?

# 5827

It is not except a reminder to the worlds

# 5828

For whoever wills among you to take a right course.

# 5829

And you do not will except that Allah wills - Lord of the worlds.

# 5830

When the sky breaks apart

# 5831

And when the stars fall, scattering,

# 5832

And when the seas are erupted

# 5833

And when the [contents of] graves are scattered,

# 5834

A soul will [then] know what it has put forth and kept back.

# 5835

O mankind, what has deceived you concerning your Lord, the Generous,

# 5836

Who created you, proportioned you, and balanced you?

# 5837

In whatever form He willed has He assembled you.

# 5838

No! But you deny the Recompense.

# 5839

# 5840

Noble and recording;

# 5841

# 5842

Indeed, the righteous will be in pleasure,

# 5843

# 5844

# 5845

# 5846

And what can make you know what is the Day of Recompense?

# 5847

Then, what can make you know what is the Day of Recompense?

# 5848

It is the Day when a soul will not possess for another soul [power to do] a thing; and the command, that Day, is [entirely] with Allah.

# 5849

Woe to those who give less [than due],

# 5850

# 5851

# 5852

Do they not think that they will be resurrected

# 5853

For a tremendous Day -

# 5854

# 5858

Woe, that Day, to the deniers,

# 5860

And none deny it except every sinful transgressor.

# 5861

# 5874

# 5875

# 5876

A spring from which those near [to Allah] drink.

# 5877

# 5878

# 5879

# 5880

# 5898

# 5907

And you see the people entering into the religion of Allah in multitudes,

# 6216

Then exalt [Him] with praise of your Lord and ask forgiveness of Him. Indeed, He is ever Accepting of repentance.

# 6217

May the hands of Abu Lahab be ruined, and ruined is he.

# 6218

His wealth will not avail him or that which he gained.

# 6219

He will [enter to] burn in a Fire of [blazing] flame

# 6220

And his wife [as well] - the carrier of firewood.

# 6221

Around her neck is a rope of [twisted] fiber.

# 6222

Say, "He is Allah, [who is] One,

# 6223

Allah, the Eternal Refuge.

# 6224

He neither begets nor is born,

# 6225

Nor is there to Him any equivalent."

# 6226

Say, "I seek refuge in the Lord of daybreak

# 6227

From the evil of that which He created

# 6228

And from the evil of darkness when it settles

# 6229

And from the evil of the blowers in knots

# 6230

And from the evil of an envier when he envies."

# 6231

Say, "I seek refuge in the Lord of mankind,

# 6232

The Sovereign of mankind.

# 6233

The God of mankind,

# 6234

From the evil of the retreating whisperer -

# 6235

Who whispers [evil] into the breasts of mankind -

# 6236

From among the jinn and mankind."
